# Surrenderless ‚Äî project state (source of truth)

This document aligns Cursor, ChatGPT, and humans on **product intent**, **current reality**, and **where to invest**. It describes the repo as of its last update; verify against code when in doubt.

---

## 1. True product goal

**Surrenderless is a chat-first action assistant.** The user should eventually **only chat** with Surrenderless ‚Äî not manually hop across forms, tabs, and external sites as the primary experience. The user **chats**; the app:

- Gathers facts **conversationally**
- **Structures** the case
- **Collects and organizes** proof (screenshots, receipts, emails, and similar ‚Äî tied to the case in-app)
- **Prepares** submissions, messages, and complaints for review (in-app previews and drafts today; more automation later where feasible)
- Gets **approval**
- **Submits or queues** actions when technically (and legally) possible
- **Tracks** confirmations, filings, and follow-ups
- **Carries** the issue from beginning to end

Existing **`/justice/*`** pages (intake form, evidence page, prep surfaces, etc.) are **interim scaffolding** toward that single conversational shell ‚Äî not the final product shape.

Anything that permanently treats ‚Äúopen another tab and paste into a government form‚Äù as the final experience is **out of scope for the long-term product**, even if it is useful as an interim step.

---

## 2. Current reality

The shipped experience is **still a multi-page Consumer Justice case-management scaffold** (many prep surfaces and manual filing paths), but **navigation across hub, preview, plan, and prep surfaces now promotes AI conversational chat intake first** toward the long-term **chat-first action** goal (¬ß1): describe the issue once in chat, structure the case, review a submission preview, approve, then follow evidence, filings, tasks, and plan guidance inside the app (filing/queueing only where feasible today; much remains manual prep and external filing).


- **Stack:** Next.js (App Router), TypeScript, **Clerk** (auth), **Supabase** (persistence via service-role API routes), **REST API routes**, **session/local storage** for active case + timeline mirror.
- **UX:** Multi-page **justice** routes (`/justice/*`): **`/justice`** workspace hub (thin landing); **primary chat intake** ‚Äî **AI conversational** intake at **`/justice/chat-ai`** (¬ß2; hub/header **Chat intake** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; preview empty-state/footer **Chat intake** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; ¬ß2 **Justice-wide navigation alignment**); **step-by-step scripted** intake at **`/justice/chat`** (labeled **Step-by-step chat** where linked; **unchanged** scripted Q&A); **structured form** intake at **`/justice/intake`** (labeled **Structured form** / **Edit structured form** where linked; loads saved answers for direct field edit); action plan; **`/justice/preview`** (in-app **submission draft preview**: deterministic text from **`buildSubmissionDraftPreview.ts`** remains **source of truth / fallback**; optional **AI-assisted** draft via signed-in **`POST /api/justice/preview-draft`** (Clerk **`getUserOr401`**, **`rateLimit`**, server-only **`OPENAI_API_KEY`**, prompts from **`buildSubmissionDraftAiPrompt.ts`**); UI copy states case details are sent to **OpenAI**; AI output is **review-only**, nothing filed; **no** DB writes, schema migrations, embedded browser, or filing automation for AI; destination selector from current justice destinations; **‚ÄúI reviewed this draft‚Äù** before **Continue to action plan** ‚Üí **`/justice/plan`**), per-destination prep pages, dedicated evidence page, saved cases, **`/justice/handling`** **Handling workbench** (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî internal triage surface**), archived cases, packet (aggregate/export). **`/justice/plan`** links to **`/justice/preview`** from the **case packet** area. **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** share **`src/lib/justice/commitIntakeToSessionAndServer.ts`** and **`src/lib/justice/normalizeCompanyWebsite.ts`** on form + scripted chat (optional company website: bare domains like `amazon.com` ‚Üí `https://amazon.com`, sentinels like `none` / `n/a` ‚Üí empty string). **Create commit (default):** **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **new** **`/justice/chat-ai`** sessions ‚Äî new case id, **`case_started`**, optional **`POST /api/justice/cases`**, **`intake_completed`**, then **`router.push("/justice/preview")`** (**`/justice/plan`** after preview continue). **Update commit:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** when an active case was hydrated (¬ß2) ‚Äî preserve case id/timeline, **`PATCH`** when signed in + UUID, no **`POST`**. **`/justice/chat`** and **`/justice/chat-ai`** use **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (**`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**, **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**, **`validateContactProofForIntake`**; ¬ß2). **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** powers AI turns on **`/justice/chat-ai`** (contract unchanged; ¬ß2).
- **Justice workspace hub (`/justice`):** **`/justice`** is shipped as a **thin**, **intentionally lightweight** Consumer Justice **workspace** landing ‚Äî **not** a dashboard rewrite and **not** a replacement for **`/justice/plan`**. Copy explains that Surrenderless **organizes consumer issues into an action plan**, prepares **drafts, checklists, and records** for the user to use, and **does not file or submit complaints automatically**. Hub copy **recommends chat intake** and notes that **form intake** remains available for users who prefer the full structured form. **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** (single client mount **read-only**) renders the hub link list and, when **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** finds valid **`sessionStorage`** intake, a compact **Current case** card ‚Äî company name, category/product labels, submission-draft status from **`readTimeline`** using **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, and one primary link to **`/justice/preview`** or **`/justice/plan`** depending on **`submission_draft_reviewed`** in session timeline; the static **Continue current action plan** hub card is **omitted** in that case so the dynamic card is the only ‚Äúnext step‚Äù CTA. **Current case** display **re-refreshes client-side** when the **tab becomes visible** (`document.visibilityState === "visible"` on **`visibilitychange`**), when the **browser window regains focus** (`window` **`focus`**), and on **`storage`** (e.g. cross-tab updates to **`sessionStorage`** / shared storage) so the card is **less likely to stay stale** after **chat**, **preview**, **plan**, or other flows that mutate local intake/timeline ‚Äî still using only **existing** local helpers (**`readValidLocalJusticeIntake`**, **`readTimeline`**, **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**); **no** hub case-list **`GET`**, **no** new routes, APIs, **`rules.ts`**, commit/preview/plan semantics, schemas, timeline event **definitions**, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`**, or **`/justice/preview`** / **`/justice/plan`** behavior changes beyond their existing writes to **`sessionStorage`**. **Needs more info** chat routing on **Current case** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**; compact **Current case** readiness checklist ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**; approved next-step label + status on **Current case** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`)**. With **no** local intake, link cards are **Start with chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**), **Use step-by-step chat** (**`/justice/chat`**; ¬ß2), **Continue current action plan**, **Start with form intake**, **Saved cases**. **No** case-list **`GET`**, **no** session mutation from the hub (reads only; active-case evidence **`GET`** for chat routing ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**). **`src/app/components/Header.tsx`** global nav order is **Justice** ‚Üí **Chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) ‚Üí **Consumer case** (form intake ‚Üí **`/justice/intake`**). **No** case **`GET`** on the hub, **no** duplication of **`rules.ts`** / plan readiness / destination logic, **no** new APIs, **no** auth changes, **no** schema or new DB tables, **no** automation, **no** filing or government submission from this surface. **Hub/header ordering** for chat-first entry is **UI-only** on this surface (see next bullet). **Preview-first intake finish** (**`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`**) is documented in ¬ß5; hub remains **read-only** (no commit from hub). **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **create** vs **update** modes: ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî hydrate & update commit**.
- **Justice hub ‚Äî handling requested on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** ‚Äî **read-only**, **session-only** (with ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`)**). When valid local intake exists and **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** has **`handling_requested_at`** for **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** (via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**), the **Current case** card shows **Surrenderless handling requested** with recorded time; when **`handling_request_note`** is also in session, shows the note read-only (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestNoteReadOnly`**); when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is in session, shows **Acknowledged {time} ‚Äî internal tracking triage only** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingAcknowledgedReadOnly`**); when **`handling_requested_at`** is in session, **display-only derived queue status** via **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`** (¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**) and **View in handling workbench** ‚Üí **`/justice/handling`** appear below the **Current case** card (outside the plan/preview card link ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî active-case back-link from hub**). When **`handling_requested_at`** is absent, **no** queue status line and **no** workbench link. **In-app tracking only** copy ‚Äî Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** server case **`GET`**, **no** request/clear buttons, **no** routing changes. Refreshes on **focus**, **`storage`**, and **visibility** like the existing snapshot. **No** schema, migration, API route, queue worker, filing record, timeline **type**, or automation.
- **Justice hub ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`**, **`deriveHandlingQueueDisplayStatus`**) ‚Äî **visibility-only** slice completing **queue-status parity** across every surface that shows handling (with ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî handling requested visibility on All cases cards**, **Handling workbench ‚Äî internal triage surface**, **Packet ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**, and **Plan ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**). When the **Current case** snapshot has **`handlingRequestedAt`** / **`handling_requested_at`** (session **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`**), renders **display-only derived queue status** from existing **`handling_requested_at`** and **`handling_acknowledged_at`** / **`handlingAcknowledgedAt`** only (**no** new persisted field, **no** writes): **Queue status: Awaiting internal triage.** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is absent; **Queue status: Acknowledged for internal tracking triage only** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set. Placed below the **Current case** card (after in-card handling disclaimer content) and before **View in handling workbench** (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî active-case back-link from hub**). When **`handling_requested_at`** is absent, **no** queue status line. **Does not** change **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, request/ack/note behavior, server **`GET`**, plan/preview CTA, chat-intake hub cards, hub refresh, or workbench link. **In-app tracking only** ‚Äî Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`** row, timeline **type**, browser automation, filing automation, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.
- **Justice hub ‚Äî handled/open handling triage note on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** ‚Äî **copy-only** slice (with ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî handling requested on Current case**, **Justice hub ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**, **Approved next action ‚Äî centralized handled/open handling triage note copy**, **Saved cases ‚Äî handled/open handling triage note on All cases cards**). When the session **Current case** snapshot has **`handling_requested_at`**, no **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, and **`approved_next_action.status === "completed"`** (via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî **`showHandledOpenHandlingTriageNote`**), renders **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingHandledOpenTriageNote`** with variant **`redirect`** below **display-only** queue status and above **View in handling workbench**. **Hidden** when **`status !== "completed"`**, when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set, or when **`handling_requested_at`** is absent. **No** **Mark acknowledged** on the hub. **Does not** change queue status, workbench link, session-only read model, focus/**`visibilitychange`**/**`storage`** refresh, in-card handling display, or external-action behavior. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only ‚Äî **UI/navigation** slice (with ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî hydrate & update commit**). When valid local intake exists (**Current case** card), uses **`isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation`** from **`caseReadiness.ts`** on session intake (**no** predicate changes). When signed in and **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** is a **UUID**, **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** (same contract as saved cases/plan ‚Äî **no** new API) on mount/focus/**`visibilitychange`**/**`storage`** refresh alongside the existing snapshot refresh; array length ‚Üí saved proof/evidence count. Directly **below** the primary **Current case** preview/plan link (outside the nested card link), one outline secondary **`Link`**: when **`!isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation(intake)`** ‚Äî **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; when basics are complete, evidence count is loaded, and **`< 1`** ‚Äî **Add proof in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; when ready (**basics** + at least one saved item) ‚Äî **no** extra CTA. Active session case only ‚Äî **no** **`activateCaseInSession`**. Primary **Current case** target (**`/justice/preview`** or **`/justice/plan`**) **unchanged**. Handling blocks below the card, hub link list, saved cases, plan, chat-ai, APIs, schema, and shared readiness logic **unchanged**. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub ‚Äî Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only ‚Äî **UI/navigation** slice (with ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**, ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî compact readiness checklist on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist proof CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist basics CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA (`/justice/plan`)**). When **Current case** exists, adds compact **`<ul>`** under the primary card link and **before** existing secondary **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** buttons ‚Äî mirrors plan **Case readiness** clarity on the hub entry surface. Uses **existing** state only (**no** new API, **no** schema): **`basicsReady`** from **`isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation`** on session intake; **`evidenceCount`** after **`!evidenceLoading`** (same evidence **`GET`** as ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**); **`snapshot.reviewed`** from session **`readTimeline`** / **`submission_draft_reviewed`**. Three rows: **Basic case info: yes/not yet** ‚Äî when **`snapshot && !basicsReady`**, inline **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Evidence: yes/not yet** (or **Evidence: loading...** while **`evidenceLoading`**) ‚Äî when loaded and **`(evidenceCount ?? 0) < 1`**, inline **Add proof in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Submission draft reviewed: yes/not yet** ‚Äî when **`snapshot && !snapshot.reviewed`**, inline **Review submission draft** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`**. Same inline link classes as plan checklist CTAs. **Does not** change **`showUpdateInChat`**, **`showAddProofInChat`**, primary **Current case** card **`href`**, evidence fetch, handling blocks, or hub link list. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** API, schema, helper, plan, preview, chat-ai, or cases changes on this slice. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub ‚Äî approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only ‚Äî **visibility-only** slice (with ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî approved next-step label on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî approved next-step label/status on Active case banner (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, ¬ß2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**). In **`readSnapshotFromLocalSession`**, reuses existing **`approvedNext`** from **`readSessionApprovedNextAction(caseId)`** (**`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**); derives **`stepLabel`** from **`approvedNext?.label?.trim()`** and **`statusLabel`** from **`approvedNextActionStatusLabel(approvedNext?.status)`** (**Approved** / **Started** / **Handled**). On the **Current case** card (inside the primary plan/preview **`Link`**, after **Submission draft reviewed** / **not reviewed** and **before** in-card handling lines and **Continue to action plan** / **Continue to submission preview**), shows read-only **Next step: {label}** (bold **label**) when **`stepLabel`** exists and **Approved next action: {statusLabel}** when **`statusLabel`** exists ‚Äî small neutral **`text-xs`** styling aligned with hub card copy. **Does not** add **Open {label}**, **Record action handled**, refresh, **`GET`**, **`PATCH`**, or server **`client_state`** read on the hub. Readiness checklist, **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** CTAs, **display-only** handling queue status below the card, **View in handling workbench**, hub link list, Plan, Packet, Chat AI, Cases, APIs, and schema **unchanged** on this slice. **In-app tracking visibility only** ‚Äî Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, contacted anyone, uploaded, stored files, or taken automatic action on the user's behalf. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**.
- **Justice workspace recovery routing (`/justice` fallback):** When a Consumer Justice page **cannot hydrate or resume a usable active case** (e.g. no valid local intake and **no server row** after **`GET /api/justice/cases`**, plan **GET**/list **hydrate** failures / empty list, **`useJusticeActionPageHydration`** unable to hydrate, or analogous **missing `STORAGE_CASE_ID` / intake** escapes on routed surfaces aligned with this pattern), **`router.replace("/justice")`** or **`router.push("/justice")`** (**and matching `Link` destinations** where the same UX intent applies) lands the user on the **`/justice`** workspace hub ‚Äî the **recovery hub** for missing / **no-case** / **failed-resume** states (replacing earlier **`/justice/intake`**-only redirects for those outcomes). **`/justice`** preserves **chat-first recovery** (**Start with chat intake** is first on the hub) while **`Start with form intake`** stays one click away. **Routing / copy-only** slice: **no** changes to **`rules.ts`**, recommendation logic, destination ordering, schemas, **API** route implementations (handlers, payloads, responses), auth guards, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** or other **persistence**/session commit behavior, timeline event **semantics**, **`/justice/preview`** deterministic or AI-assisted draft **generation**, filing automation, or filing/submission flows.
- **Chat-first navigation promotion (UI only on hub/header):** **`/justice`** workspace and **`Header.tsx`** emphasize **AI conversational chat intake** first ‚Äî **Justice** ‚Üí **Chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) ‚Üí **Consumer case** (**`/justice/intake`**) in the header; **Start with chat intake** is the **first** hub card (**`/justice/chat-ai`**). A second hub card, **Use step-by-step chat**, links to **scripted** **`/justice/chat`** (¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî step-by-step chat fallback**). **`/justice/chat`** remains **scripted** Q&A (not LLM-driven); **scripted chat behavior is unchanged** on this slice. **`/justice/chat-ai`** page copy presents conversational intake as the primary **Your consumer case** path (not a separate ‚Äúprototype‚Äù label). **Preview-first intake finish:** after successful commit, **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** **`router.push`** **`/justice/preview`**; users reach **`/justice/plan`** through the existing preview page (**`submission_draft_reviewed`** tracking unchanged). **Navigation slice only:** **no** new APIs, **no** prompt/parser changes, **no** LLM behavior changes, **no** auth changes on scripted chat, **no** schema or DB changes, **no** Supabase changes, **no** **`caseReadiness.ts`** changes, **no** plan **`rules.ts`** logic changes, **no** preview/plan behavior changes beyond existing flows. (Intake **commit** and **hydration** behavior for **`/justice/chat-ai`** are documented in ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî hydrate & update commit**.)
- **Chat intake ‚Äî shared `JusticeIntake` builder (scripted `/justice/chat` + AI `/justice/chat-ai` + structured alignment):** **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** centralizes **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** defaults and conversion: **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts()`**, forward **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** (trim strings, **`normalizeCompanyWebsite`** on scripted/AI paths that use it, merge **`money_amount`** + **`desired_resolution`** into **`money_involved`** with separator **` ‚Äî Desired outcome: `**, contact fields only when **`already_contacted === "yes"`**, optional **`consumer_us_state`**), and reverse **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (hydrate saved **`JusticeIntake`** from **`sessionStorage`** ‚Äî conservative split of **`money_involved`** on that separator or hyphen variant, safe contact enums, **`already_contacted`** only **`yes`** when stored as yes). **Scripted** **`/justice/chat`** and **AI** **`/justice/chat-ai`** both produce the **same `JusticeIntake`** shape before commit. **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`** imports shared **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (re-exported) instead of duplicating defaults. **Post-intake rail:** build intake ‚Üí **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** (**`create`** or **`update`** on chat-ai when applicable) ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** ‚Üí **`/justice/plan`**. **Still unchanged on this slice:** **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, filing/evidence APIs, Supabase schema, **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** contract, auto-filing/submission automation (¬ß1).
- **Chat intake ‚Äî shared contact-proof validation (scripted `/justice/chat` + AI `/justice/chat-ai`):** **`validateContactProofForIntake`** in **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (same module as the builder): when **`already_contacted === "yes"`**, **`contact_proof_type`** **`none`** or **`ticket`** requires non-empty **`contact_proof_text`** with fixed error strings (**‚ÄúDescribe your contact attempt before continuing.‚Äù** / **‚ÄúEnter the ticket or case number before continuing.‚Äù**). Used by **scripted** chat and **AI** chat before commit (**`create`** or **`update`**). **Validation rules unchanged** on hydrate/update slice; **no** change to **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, or intake-chat API.
- **AI intake chat API (`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`):** **`src/app/api/justice/intake-chat/route.ts`** with **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** and **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`**. **Request:** `{ user_message, parts: BuildJusticeIntakeParts, conversation_history?: { role: "user" | "assistant"; content: string }[] }` ‚Äî one user turn plus current partial parts and optional capped history. **Response:** `{ assistantMessage, parts }` ‚Äî updated **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (pre-commit; not full **`JusticeIntake`** until client runs **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**). **Security:** same envelope as **`preview-draft`** ‚Äî **`getUserOr401`**, **`rateLimit`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY`** server-only, bounded body, JSON validation/clamping, OpenAI **`json_object`** response parsed before return. **No** Supabase / DB writes, **no** timeline writes, **no** case creation, **no** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** in the API. Consumed by **`/justice/chat-ai`** (¬ß2). **Scripted `/justice/chat`** unchanged.
- **AI chat intake (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** ‚Äî **primary AI conversational intake** UI (hub/header **Chat intake** and **Start with chat intake** ‚Üí here; plan **Update in chat** ‚Üí here; ¬ß2 **Chat-first navigation promotion** / **Justice-wide navigation alignment**). **Separate route** from **scripted** **`/justice/chat`** (scripted page **unchanged**; linked as **Use step-by-step chat**). **`/justice/intake`** remains the **structured form fallback** (**Edit structured form**). **Clerk** sign-in required (**`JusticeActionResumeSignInPrompt`** when signed out). On mount, **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** (¬ß2 **hydrate & update commit**): if valid **`STORAGE_INTAKE`** exists, **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** seeds **`parts`**, **Recap** shows the loaded case immediately, assistant copy explains the case is loaded and the user can describe changes; otherwise fresh **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts()`** + new-case greeting. When **`approved_next_action`** is present, **Current action tracking** in **Recap** (¬ß2). Local **`messages`** and **`parts`**; each send calls **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** with **`{ user_message, parts, conversation_history }`** (history = prior UI messages only; in-flight send guard ¬ß2; API error-copy polish ¬ß2). Shows assistant replies, compact **Recap** (including **Proof / evidence** guidance ¬ß2 and **Current action tracking** when applicable), OpenAI disclosure. **Continue to submission preview** blocked until basics present (¬ß2 preview-readiness polish); **evidence not required** before preview. When complete: **`validateContactProofForIntake`** ‚Üí **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** ‚Üí **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** with **`mode: "update"`** when hydrated from an existing case, else **`create`** (**`commitLogLabel`**: **`justice chat-ai`**) ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** ‚Üí **`/justice/plan`**. **Not filing automation** ‚Äî same review/preview/plan rail as before. **Unchanged:** **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** contract, prompt/parser, **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, filing/evidence **APIs**, Supabase schema, scripted **`/justice/chat`** Q&A.

Copy frames this as the **chat-first workflow** (next step in the same case), not a separate manual detour. - **Chat AI intake ‚Äî hydrate & update commit:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** is the in-app **Update in chat** path for an **active local case** (e.g. from **`/justice/plan`**, **Saved cases**, or hub ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**, ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**). **Hydration:** one-time mount read via **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** ‚Üí **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** in **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (shared with scripted/structured alignment); baseline **`parts`** snapshot for session change summary ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî session change summary (Update in chat)**. **Active case** orientation banner when hydrated ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî active case context banner (Update in chat)**; compact readiness checklist on **Update in chat** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; read-only approved next-step label/status on **Active case** banner when **`approvedNextAction`** exists ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî approved next-step label/status on Active case banner (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**. **Commit:** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **`mode: "update"`** preserves **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, does **not** call **`newCaseId()`**, does **not** **`clearTimelineForNewCase`**, does **not** append **`case_started`**, does **not** clear FTC/mock keys, does **not** fire **`intake_completed`**, does **not** **`POST /api/justice/cases`**; writes **`STORAGE_INTAKE`**; when signed in and case id is a **UUID**, **`PATCH /api/justice/cases/[id]`** with `{ intake, timeline }` (same pattern as merchant save). **Create** **`mode`** (default) unchanged for new intake and for **`/justice/intake`** / **`/justice/chat`**. **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** returns **`CommitIntakeResult`** **`{ caseId, serverPersisted }`** ‚Äî **create** sets **`serverPersisted`** when signed-in **`POST /api/justice/cases`** succeeds with **`id`**; **update** sets **`serverPersisted`** when **`PATCH`** succeeds (callers may ignore; ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)** uses it before flushing staged proof). **No** new timeline event type for ‚Äúintake updated‚Äù on this slice. **Limitations:** **`/justice/intake`** submit still uses **create** only (editing loaded session can still spawn a duplicate case ‚Äî pre-existing); signed-out or non-UUID session ids get local intake update only (no server PATCH); **no** filing/submission automation.

- **Handling workbench ‚Äî completed-unacknowledged handling count in Awaiting helper (`/justice/handling`):** **`src/app/justice/handling/page.tsx`** only ‚Äî **discoverability-only** slice (with ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî align Awaiting internal triage with Saved cases Needs attention**). From **`allHandlingItems`**, computes **`completedUnacknowledgedCount`** for cases where **`handling_requested_at`** is set, **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is absent, and **`approved_next_action.status === "completed"`**. When count **> 0**, extends the existing **Awaiting internal triage** helper with one line: **{N} handled approved action(s) still have an open handling request ‚Äî acknowledge from your action plan or chat intake.** Those cases **remain excluded** from **Awaiting** and **Saved cases** **Needs attention**; they stay visible on **All cases** (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî handling requested visibility on All cases cards**). Per-case identification ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî read-only handled/open-request rows under Awaiting**. **No** third top-level workbench section, **no** **Mark acknowledged** on workbench for those cases, **no** change to **Awaiting** or **Acknowledged** membership, active **Awaiting** per-card CTAs, queue status, notes, disclaimers, pagination, APIs, **Needs attention** rules, or chat/plan/cases ack behavior. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**; Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone.
- **Handling workbench ‚Äî read-only handled/open-request rows under Awaiting (`/justice/handling`):** **`src/app/justice/handling/page.tsx`** only ‚Äî **discoverability + navigation** slice (with ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî completed-unacknowledged handling count in Awaiting helper** and **Handling workbench ‚Äî align Awaiting internal triage with Saved cases Needs attention**). From **`allHandlingItems`**, builds **`completedUnacknowledgedItems`** with the same membership as **`completedUnacknowledgedCount`**: **`handling_requested_at`** set, **`handling_acknowledged_at`** absent, **`approved_next_action.status === "completed"`** (handled approved action with an open handling request). When **`completedUnacknowledgedItems.length > 0`**, renders a **nested** block **under** **Awaiting internal triage** (below existing **Awaiting** helper/count copy) ‚Äî **not** a third top-level section. Subheading **Handled ‚Äî open handling request**; section helper: **These cases are not in Awaiting or Saved cases Needs attention. Mark acknowledged from the action plan or chat intake. Surrenderless has not filed, submitted, or queued anything externally.** Reuses **`HandlingWorkbenchCaseCard`** with **`showMarkAcknowledged={false}`** and **`compactNavigation`** (**Open action plan**, **Update in chat** only ‚Äî **no** **Open case packet** or **Open approved step** on these rows). Cards show the same read-only handling fields (label/company, product, approved-action status, **Surrenderless handling requested**, recorded time, optional **`handling_request_note`**, **display-only** queue status, disclaimer). Per-card handled/open triage note ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî handled/open redirect note on nested Handled ‚Äî open cards**. **Session highlight** (**Current case in this browser**) applies the same as other workbench cards. **Mark acknowledged** remains **only** on active **Awaiting** rows and from **`/justice/plan`** / **`/justice/chat-ai`** (and **Saved cases** **Needs attention**) for these cases; after ack from plan or chat, rows leave the nested list and appear in **Acknowledged** after reload. **Does not** change **Awaiting** membership, **Acknowledged** membership, **Saved cases** **Needs attention** rules, **`GET` + merge + `PATCH`** semantics, queue-status derivation, pagination, **`handling_request_note`** edit/clear, or external-action copy on other surfaces. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**; Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone.
- **Handling workbench ‚Äî handled/open redirect note on nested Handled ‚Äî open cards (`/justice/handling`):** **`src/app/justice/handling/page.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** ‚Äî **copy-only** slice (with ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî read-only handled/open-request rows under Awaiting**, **Approved next action ‚Äî centralized handled/open handling triage note copy**). In **`HandlingWorkbenchCaseCard`**, when **`handling_requested_at`**, no **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, and **`status === "completed"`** (**`showHandledOpenHandlingTriageNote`**), renders **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingHandledOpenTriageNote`** with variant **`redirect`** (**`HANDLING_HANDLED_OPEN_TRIAGE_NOTE_REDIRECT`**) after **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`** and before **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingAcknowledgedReadOnly`** and the generic disclaimer / nav buttons. Applies to nested **Handled ‚Äî open handling request** rows (**`compactNavigation`**); **not** shown on active **Awaiting internal triage** cards (**`status !== "completed"`**) or **Acknowledged** cards (**`handling_acknowledged_at`** set). **No** per-card **Mark acknowledged** on nested rows; section heading + section helper under **Awaiting** **unchanged**. **Does not** change **Awaiting** / **Acknowledged** membership (**`isHandlingAwaitingTriageApprovedNextAction`**), **Mark acknowledged** on active **Awaiting** rows, **Open action plan** / **Update in chat** on nested rows, refetch on focus (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî refetch active cases on window focus**), session highlight (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî current browser-session case highlight**), **Saved cases** behavior, APIs, schema, persistence, or hub/packet/plan/chat/cases handled/open notes. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.

Complements ¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî internal triage surface** and **Handling workbench ‚Äî active-case back-link from plan and chat-ai** so users returning from a case surface can spot the active session case in the list ‚Äî **in-app tracking only**; Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone.

Keeps **`refreshSessionCaseIdFromStorage`** on the same events so **Current case in this browser** stays aligned. **Purpose:** when the user returns to an open workbench tab after **Mark acknowledged** on **`/justice/plan`** or **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **Awaiting internal triage**, nested **Handled ‚Äî open handling request**, and **Acknowledged** rebucket from fresh **`client_state`** without a full page reload. **Workbench-local Mark acknowledged** still updates **`cases`** immediately via **`applyAcknowledgedHandlingToCaseRow`** ‚Äî refocus refetch is additive, not required for on-page ack. **Does not** change UI, copy, routes, APIs, schema, persistence, **`isHandlingAwaitingTriageApprovedNextAction`** / nested handled membership rules, per-card CTAs, queue status, notes, disclaimers, **Mark acknowledged** semantics, plan/chat/cases ack, or external-action behavior. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation; Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone.

- **Packet ‚Äî Open approved step marks started tracking (`/justice/packet`):** **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`** only ‚Äî **behavior** slice mirroring ¬ß2 **Approved next action started (`/justice/plan`)** (with ¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî approved next action started surfaced (`/justice/packet`)**, ¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**). When the packet is approved and **`approved_next_action.status`** is **`"approved"`** (not **`started`** or **`completed`**), **Open {label}** in the **Packet approved for next action** inner card is a **`<button>`** calling page-local **`handleApprovedNextActionOpen`**: builds **`approved_next_action`** with existing **`label`** / **`href`**, sets **`status: "started"`** and **`started_at`** (preserves **`approved_at`**), merges tracking fields via **`mergeApprovedNextActionTrackingFields`**, writes **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** and **`justice_prepared_packet_approved_v1`** session maps, updates React state, **`await`**s page-local **`persistApprovedNextActionClientState`** (**`GET` + **`mergeClientStateWithApprovedNextAction`** + **`PATCH`** existing **`/api/justice/cases/[id]`** **`client_state`**) for signed-in **UUID** cases, then **`router.push`** to the approved **`href`**. If already **`completed`**, navigates only ‚Äî **no** status downgrade. When **`started`** or **`completed`**, **Open {label}** remains plain **`Link`** navigation ‚Äî **does not** downgrade **`started`** ‚Üí **`approved`** or **`completed`** to a lower state. **Does not** change approval checkpoint, **`handleApprovePreparedPacket`**, post-approval explainer copy, **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming`** gates, packet body, copy/download/print, **`JusticeFilingRecords`**, **`JusticeCaseTasks`**, prep routes, APIs, schema, **`rules.ts`**, plan, preview, chat-ai, hub, cases. **In-app tracking only** ‚Äî Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.
- **Packet ‚Äî handling requested visibility (prepared-action area) (`/justice/packet`):** **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** ‚Äî **read-only mirror** of plan/chat/cases (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Surrenderless handling requested**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî handling requested in Current action tracking**, **Saved cases ‚Äî handling requested visibility on All cases cards**). When **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming`** is active and **`client_state.approved_next_action.handling_requested_at`** is set (hydrated via **`hydrateApprovedNextActionForDisplay`** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**), **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestedReadOnly`** shows **Surrenderless handling requested**, recorded time, optional **`handling_request_note`**, and optional **Acknowledged {time} ‚Äî internal tracking triage only** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set; when **`handling_requested_at`** is set, **display-only derived queue status** via **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`** (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**) and **View in handling workbench** ‚Üí **`/justice/handling`** (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî active-case back-link from packet**) appear in the handling fragment. - **Packet ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status (`/justice/packet`):** **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`**, **`deriveHandlingQueueDisplayStatus`**) ‚Äî **visibility-only** slice aligning packet with ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî handling requested visibility on All cases cards**, **Handling workbench ‚Äî internal triage surface**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**, and **Plan ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**. When **`approved_next_action.handling_requested_at`** is set (hydrated **`approved_next_action`** in the prepared-action handling fragment), renders **display-only derived queue status** from existing **`handling_requested_at`** and **`handling_acknowledged_at`** only (**no** new persisted field, **no** writes): **Queue status: Awaiting internal triage.** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is absent; **Queue status: Acknowledged for internal tracking triage only** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set. When **`handling_requested_at`** is absent, **no** queue status line. **Does not** change packet approval, timeline, **`JusticeFilingRecords`**, **`JusticeCaseTasks`**, follow-up UI, workbench link, or other packet copy. **In-app tracking only** ‚Äî Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`** row, timeline **type**, browser automation, filing automation, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.

In the prepared-action handling fragment when **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming`** is active and hydrated **`approved_next_action`** has **`handling_requested_at`**, no **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, and **`status === "completed"`**, renders **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingHandledOpenTriageNote`** with variant **`redirect`** after **display-only** queue status (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**) and before **View in handling workbench** (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî active-case back-link from packet**). **Hidden** when **`status !== "completed"`**, when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set, or when **`handling_requested_at`** is absent. **No** **Mark acknowledged** on packet. **Does not** change **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestedReadOnly`**, queue status, workbench link, packet approval/**PATCH**, timeline, filings, tasks, hydrate paths, or external-action behavior. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Approved next action target (`client_state` ‚Äî packet + plan):** **`src/lib/justice/types.ts`** (**`JusticeApprovedNextAction`**, **`approved_next_action`** on **`JusticeCaseClientState`**), **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`**, **`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`**. On **`/justice/packet`** approval (when prepared framing is active), Surrenderless stores **both** packet-approved state and **which in-app step** was approved for, using existing **`justice_cases.client_state`** only: **`approved_next_action`** with optional **`label`**, **`href`**, **`status: "approved"`**, **`approved_at`** (ISO). Target is derived at approve time from the same page-local **`pickPreparedNextAction`** logic as **`/justice/plan`** (contact state + first **`recommended`** / **`available`** destination with **`internalRoute`** via **`computeJusticeDestinations`** ‚Äî e.g. merchant/company contact **`/justice/merchant`** or a prep route; **`href`** falls back to **`/justice/packet`** when no prep route). **Hydrate:** packet **`GET /api/justice/cases/[id]`** restores **`approved_next_action`** (including **`started`** when present) after refresh; syncs **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** session map when server has data. **Plan:** existing case **`GET`** hydrate paths read **`approved_next_action`** and surface the **exact stored label/href** in approved callouts when the user returns from packet ‚Äî not a recomputed destination. **Session fallback:** **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** for local / non-UUID. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or new timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted automatically. **Interim scaffolding** toward ¬ß1 **chat-first ‚Üí prepare ‚Üí approve ‚Üí start/track** ‚Äî remembers approval **intent**, not execution.
- **Approved next action started (`/justice/plan` + `/justice/packet` + `/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`** (primary write on plan); **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`** (write on packet **Open {label}** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî Open approved step marks started tracking (`/justice/packet`)**); **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** (write on chat **Open {label}** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Open approved step marks started in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**); **`src/lib/justice/types.ts`** ‚Äî **`JusticeApprovedNextAction.status`** includes **`"started"`** with optional **`started_at`** (full union **`"approved" | "started" | "completed"`** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Approved next action completed / handled**; packet surfaces **`started`** on hydrate ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî approved next action started surfaced**). After return/refresh, callouts read **Next action started** / **Opened for next step** when **`status === "started"`**. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted automatically. **Interim scaffolding** toward ¬ß1 **prepare ‚Üí approve ‚Üí start/track**.

- **Approved next action shared state helpers (`approvedNextActionState.ts`):** **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionState.ts`** centralizes **`approved_next_action`** parsing from unknown **`client_state`** / session values (**`parseApprovedNextAction`**, **`parseApprovedNextActionFromClientState`**, **`parseJusticeCaseClientState`**), status display labels (**`approvedNextActionStatusLabel`** ‚Äî **Approved** / **Started** / **Handled**), handling awaiting-triage membership (**`isHandlingAwaitingTriageApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Approved next action ‚Äî shared handling awaiting-triage membership predicate**), follow-up clearing (**`clearFollowUpFromApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî removes **`follow_up_needed`** while preserving **`outcome_note`**, **`follow_up_at`**, **`handling_requested_at`**, **`handling_request_note`**, **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, **`status`**, **`href`**, **`label`**, **`approved_at`**, **`started_at`**, **`completed_at`**, and other fields), handling-request note updates (**`applyHandlingRequestNoteToApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî sets or clears **`handling_request_note`** only), cleared-follow-up **`client_state`** merge (**`mergeClientStateWithClearedFollowUp`** ‚Äî preserves **`prepared_packet_approved`**), plan/packet persist merge (**`mergeClientStateWithApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî preserves prior fields unless incoming action omits **`handling_request_note`** intentionally; forces **`prepared_packet_approved`** on plan persist), session + server resolve (**`resolveApprovedNextAction`** ‚Äî merges **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** with **`client_state`**; **does not downgrade** **`completed`** ‚Üí **`started`** ‚Üí **`approved`**), display hydrate (**`hydrateApprovedNextActionForDisplay`** ‚Äî coalesces **`handling_acknowledged_at`** from session, resolved action, and raw **`client_state`** for plan/chat/packet UI), tracking-field preserve on persist (**`mergeApprovedNextActionTrackingFields`** ‚Äî keeps **`handling_requested_at`** / **`handling_acknowledged_at`** when a patch omits them), and session map read/write (**`STORAGE_APPROVED_NEXT_ACTION_V1`** / **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`**). **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **`/justice/cases`**, **`/justice/plan`**, and **`/justice/packet`** import these helpers (chat-ai **Current action tracking** / **Open {label}** when **`approved`** / **Record action handled for now** / **completed-step clarity** / **Mark follow-up handled** / **Request Surrenderless handling** / **Mark acknowledged** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî approved next action display hydrate**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Open approved step marks started in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî record action handled in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî completed-step clarity in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî handling requested in Current action tracking**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî acknowledge handling request in Current action tracking**; cases **Needs attention** / **Clear follow-up** / **All cases** **`CaseApprovedNextActionTracking`** ‚Äî **Next step: {label}** when set (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî approved next-step label on All cases cards**), **`handling_requested_at`** visibility (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî handling requested visibility on All cases cards**); plan **approved** / **started** / **handled** / outcome follow-up / **Request Surrenderless handling** / **Mark acknowledged** persist (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî acknowledge handling request in Surrenderless handling UI**); packet **approval** hydrate and return-to-plan). Reduces duplicated parsing/resolving/merge logic across all four surfaces and keeps handling request/note/ack visible when session and server disagree. **No** schema, migration, API route, queue worker, automation, filing behavior, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued, or contacted automatically. **No** schema, migration, API route, queue worker, automation, filing behavior, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued, or contacted automatically.

When **Update in chat** loads a case, **Current action tracking** seeds from **`hydrateApprovedNextActionForDisplay(caseId)`** immediately; for signed-in **UUID** cases, after **`GET /api/justice/cases/[id]`**, **`hydrateApprovedNextActionForDisplay(caseId, client_state)`** coalesces **`handling_requested_at`**, **`handling_request_note`**, and **`handling_acknowledged_at`** with session/server/raw **`client_state`** (status merge still via **`resolveApprovedNextAction`** inside the helper; **does not downgrade** **`completed`** ‚Üí **`started`** ‚Üí **`approved`**).
