The preview uses the **same deterministic** issuer letter as **`/justice/payment-dispute`**, via **`src/lib/justice/buildPaymentDisputeBankLetter.ts`** (**`buildBankLetter`**, **`buildDefaultPaymentDisputeDraft`** for default checklist fields from **`JusticeIntake`**). The preview is **collapsed by default** and **truncated** in the UI to reduce accidental PII exposure; **`/justice/payment-dispute`** remains the **full** checklist, **Copy text**, and **save** flow (**`payment_dispute_draft`** + timeline via existing **PATCH** case behavior). **No** sending automation, **no** opening external bank or card issuer websites from this slice, **no** task creation, **no** automatic evidence rows, **no** automatic filing records, **no** API route or handler changes, **no** changes to **`/justice/preview`** or **`submission_draft_reviewed`** tracking, **no** change to the merchant-message plan preview behavior, **no** filing automation, **no** embedded browser, **no** schema changes, **no** new DB tables.
- **Saved evidence ‚Äî plan preview:** **`/justice/plan`** surfaces **saved evidence metadata** under the **Evidence / proof** card when the user is **signed in** and **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id=...`** returns at least one row (same fetch already used for **case readiness** / evidence count). The block is **collapsed by default** (`<details>`) and shows **metadata only**: **title**, **evidence type**, optional **evidence date**, and a **short truncated description** (no `source_url` in the preview list; still **no file uploads** in the product). A **Manage evidence** link goes to **`/justice/evidence`** for full add/edit/delete. When **no** rows after load, shows **No saved proof notes on this case yet.** + **Add proof in chat ‚Üí** **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Add evidence** ‚Üí **`/justice/evidence`** **unchanged** (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî proof readiness continuity after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**). **`/justice/evidence`** remains the **only** full evidence CRUD page; **evidence save behavior** and **`POST /api/justice/evidence`** are **unchanged**; successful **create** still appends **`evidence_added`** to **`justice_cases.timeline`** via existing server logic. **No** automatic evidence creation, **no** task creation, **no** API changes, **no** changes to packet, merchant, payment, preview/review, or filing surfaces beyond this plan UI, **no** filing automation, **no** embedded browser, **no** schema changes, **no** new DB tables.
- **Saved filings ‚Äî plan preview:** **`/justice/plan`** surfaces **saved filing record metadata** under the **Filing records** card when the user is **signed in** and **`GET /api/justice/filings?case_id=...`** returns at least one row (same **`filings`** state already loaded for **case readiness**). The block is **collapsed by default** (`<details>`) and **metadata-only**: **destination**, optional **filed date** (`filed_at` when present), **truncated confirmation** snippet, **truncated notes** snippet ‚Äî it **intentionally omits `filing_url`** on the plan card to reduce nudging users toward external sites from the plan surface. Copy links to **`/justice/packet`** to **add or edit** filing records (**`JusticeFilingRecords`** on the packet page); **`/justice/packet`** remains the **full** packet bundle plus **filing record** management. **Filing** save/edit/delete behavior and **`POST` / `PATCH` / `DELETE`** filing APIs are **unchanged**; **`POST /api/justice/filings`** still appends **`filing_recorded`** to **`justice_cases.timeline`**. **No** automatic filing rows, **no** inline filing form on **`/justice/plan`**, **no** task creation, **no** API changes, **no** changes to packet/merchant/payment/evidence/preview/review behavior beyond this plan UI, **no** filing automation, **no** embedded browser, **no** schema changes, **no** new DB tables.
- **FTC practice ‚Äî plan preview:** **`/justice/plan`** surfaces a compact **FTC practice preview** inside **Step 3 ‚Äî Escalate to FTC** when that **FTC fallback** Step 3 path is active (i.e. not when **CFPB**, **FCC**, or **DOT** is the primary Step 3), **FTC is unlocked** (same gating as the existing FTC CTA in **`rules.ts` / `computeFtcUnlocked`**) and **FTC practice is not already completed** (session mock-completion flag not set). The block uses **existing `JusticeIntake`** on the plan page only ‚Äî **no** new fetches. It is **collapsed by default** (`<details>`) and **metadata-only**: **company name**, **issue / problem category**, optional **money amount**, optional **date / order date**, optional **reply email**, and a **truncated complaint / story** summary. Copy states clearly that the flow is **practice-only**, **not** a real government filing, **nothing** is submitted to the FTC automatically, and there is **no** external FTC submission from this slice. A **Continue to practice FTC form** link goes to **`/justice/ftc-review`** for the full internal practice review and optional autofill. **`/justice/ftc-review`** remains the **full** practice review / autofill page; **`/mock/ftc-complaint`** remains **internal mock QA only**. **No** real FTC filing, **no** **`/api/submit-form`** behavior changes, **no** API changes, **no** timeline behavior changes from this preview alone, **no** automatic filings, evidence, or tasks, **no** filing automation, **no** embedded browser, **no** schema changes or new DB tables. **Merchant**, **payment**, **evidence**, and **filing** plan previews remain **unchanged**.
- **BBB / State AG / CFPB / FCC / DOT / demand letter (`small_claims`) ‚Äî plan destination previews:** **`/justice/plan`** surfaces **compact**, **collapsed** (`<details>`) **metadata-only** previews on the **Better Business Bureau**, **State Attorney General**, **CFPB**, **FCC**, **USDOT / aviation**, and **Small claims / demand letter** (**`small_claims`**) rows in **‚ÄúOther places this may go‚Äù** when each destination is present with **`internalRoute`** (same **`computeJusticeDestinations`** / row shape as before). Previews sit **in the row before/near** the existing **Open** controls; **destination ordering**, **badges**, **`Open`** **`href`s**, and **analytics** (`bbb_prep_opened`, `state_ag_prep_opened`, `cfpb_prep_opened`, `fcc_prep_opened`, **`dot_prep_opened`**, **`demand_letter_prep_opened`** on link click) follow the shipped pattern. **BBB, State AG, CFPB, FCC, FTC, payment dispute, and merchant** destination rows behave as before; **DOT** receives **`internalRoute: "/justice/dot"`** when aviation hints match (**`dotLikelyRelevant`**); **`small_claims`** receives **`internalRoute: "/justice/demand-letter"`** (row **label** remains **‚ÄúSmall claims / demand letter‚Äù**), keeps **`status: "later"`**, and is **not** promoted to **primary Step 3**. Metadata: **company**, **issue / category**, optional **money**, optional **order/payment date**, optional **`consumer_us_state`** on the **State AG** row only, **merchant contact** summary/outcome when documented, and **truncated story** ‚Äî **no** full complaint draft text on the plan. Copy: **manual prep**; **Surrenderless does not file** automatically; one-line guidance to copy the full draft on **`/justice/bbb`**, **`/justice/state-ag`**, **`/justice/cfpb`**, **`/justice/fcc`**, the **DOT aviation prep** page, or the **demand letter prep** page as applicable. **`/justice/bbb`**, **`/justice/state-ag`**, **`/justice/cfpb`**, **`/justice/fcc`**, **`/justice/dot`**, and **`/justice/demand-letter`** are manual prep surfaces (no automatic filing from the app). **No** new backend APIs for this slice, **no** tasks, **no** automatic filings or evidence, **no** new timeline **types** from opening the prep page alone, **no** filing automation, **no** embedded browser, **no** schema or new DB tables, **no** changes to **`submission_draft_reviewed`** / preview-review tracking. **Merchant**, **payment**, **evidence**, **filing**, **FTC** (fallback Step 3), and **final follow-up** plan previews remain **unchanged** except where **DOT** primary Step 3 applies (see next bullet).
- **Demand letter (`/justice/demand-letter`) ‚Äî manual prep slice:** **`/justice/demand-letter`** is shipped as a **manual** demand-letter prep page reached through the existing **`small_claims`** destination row labeled **‚ÄúSmall claims / demand letter.‚Äù** The page provides **copy-ready** neutral demand-letter text (from **`JusticeIntake`** only), **case summary**, **company / person** info, **what happened**, **requested resolution**, **evidence checklist**, **`JusticeSavedEvidenceList`**, and **user-driven** **`JusticeFilingRecords`**. It is **not legal advice**; it does **not** determine whether the user **qualifies for small claims**; it does **not** file, submit, embed court sites, or automate court or government actions. Users are told to **verify deadlines, dollar limits, venue / jurisdiction, service rules, and court rules** with **official or local court** resources. **No** schema changes, **no** new DB tables, **no** automatic tasks, **no** automatic filings, **no** automatic evidence, **no** court filing, **no** embedded browser, **no** filing automation. **Existing** merchant, payment, evidence, filing, FTC, final follow-up, BBB, State AG, CFPB, FCC, and DOT behavior **remains unchanged**.
- **DOT / USDOT aviation ‚Äî manual prep page and plan priority:** **`/justice/dot`** is shipped as a **manual** USDOT / aviation consumer complaint prep page: **copy-ready** DOT aviation complaint text (from existing **`JusticeIntake`** fields only), **evidence checklist**, **`JusticeSavedEvidenceList`**, and **user-driven** **`JusticeFilingRecords`** ‚Äî **no** automatic filing rows, **no** automatic evidence, **no** task creation. Surrenderless **does not file** automatically, **does not embed** the DOT website, and **does not submit** to any government system; there are **no** new APIs, **no** schema changes, **no** new DB tables, **no** embedded browser, and **no** filing automation for this surface. In **`src/lib/justice/rules.ts`**, when DOT/aviation text hints match (**`dotLikelyRelevant`** / **`matchesDotHints`**), the USDOT/aviation destination includes **`internalRoute: "/justice/dot"`** (unresolved action plans). **`/justice/plan`** Step 3 escalation priority is **CFPB ‚Üí FCC ‚Üí DOT ‚Üí FTC fallback**; for aviation / flight / refund / cancellation / baggage-related cases **without** CFPB or FCC primacy, **DOT is the primary Step 3** (**‚ÄúStep 3 ‚Äî Escalate to DOT‚Äù**), with CTA **‚ÄúPrepare DOT aviation complaint‚Äù** ‚Üí **`/justice/dot`**, manual-prep-only copy, and **`dot_prep_opened`** analytics from the Step 3 link (**`from: "plan_step3"`**). **FTC** remains available as a **secondary** path (e.g. **‚ÄúOther places this may go‚Äù** and **`/justice/ftc-review`**) rather than the **primary** Step 3 for those aviation-focused cases. **Existing** merchant contact, payment dispute, evidence, filing, final follow-up, BBB, State AG, CFPB, and FCC behavior is **unchanged** except **DOT** may take **primary Step 3** when relevant and appears in **destinations** with **`internalRoute`** and the **collapsed** plan preview as above. **Demand letter** (**`small_claims`**, **`/justice/demand-letter`**) is separate ‚Äî see the preceding bullet ‚Äî and is **not** promoted to primary Step 3.
- **Persistence:** When signed in, a **`justice_cases`** row holds intake, timeline JSON, optional payment-dispute draft and client state; **evidence**, **filing records**, and **follow-up tasks** live in child tables.
- **Parallel legacy surface:** Root home (`/`) and dashboard-style flows (e.g. generic ask, form-fill demos, task logs, USPS demo) are **not** the Consumer Justice product; they share the repo.

---

## 3. What existing systems should be reused

Do **not** throw away these; they are the right backbone for a chat-first evolution:

| System | Role |
|--------|------|
| **`justice_cases`** | Canonical case: `intake`, `timeline`, `payment_dispute_draft`, `client_state`, `case_label`, `archived_at`. |
| **Timeline** | Append-only-style events (client session + server JSONB); server idempotent append for resource-linked events. |
| **Evidence** | Metadata rows (no file blobs in MVP); types/labels in `src/lib/justice/evidence.ts`. **`/justice/plan`** (`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`): when signed in and saved rows exist, reuses the same **`GET /api/justice/evidence`** response as readiness to show a **collapsed** ‚ÄúSaved evidence‚Äù preview (title, type, optional date, truncated description) + link to **`/justice/evidence`** ‚Äî **no** API or save-behavior changes. |
| **Filing records** | User-tracked external/manual filings; confirmation numbers, URLs, notes. **`/justice/plan`** (`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`): when signed in and saved rows exist, reuses the same **`GET /api/justice/filings`** response as readiness for a **collapsed** ‚ÄúSaved filings‚Äù preview (destination, optional filed date, truncated confirmation and notes; **no `filing_url`**) + link to **`/justice/packet`** for full **`JusticeFilingRecords`** CRUD ‚Äî **no** API or save-behavior changes. |
| **Follow-up tasks** | Titles, text due dates, notes, completion; ties to timeline. |
| **Readiness** | `src/lib/justice/caseReadiness.ts` and plan UX (‚Äúready to escalate‚Äù vs ‚Äúneeds more info‚Äù). |
| **Saved cases** | `src/app/justice/cases/page.tsx` + `GET/PATCH` case APIs (**`client_state`** on list **GET**); search/filter/sort (client-side). **Start new case** clears local Justice session (**`clearLocalJusticeSession`**) and routes to **`/justice`** workspace hub (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî Start new case routing**). **Needs attention** uses **`filteredSortedCases`** like **All cases** ‚Äî open **tasks** (**Open case**) plus **`approved_next_action.follow_up_needed`** cards (**Open action**, **Clear follow-up**; ¬ß2 **Needs attention opens approved action surface**, **Saved cases ‚Äî clear Needs attention follow-up**) with user-paced timing labels (¬ß2 **Approved next action follow-up timing**). Per-card **readiness helper** only when **Needs more info**; **Ready to escalate** keeps status + stats (¬ß2 **readiness status hints**). **All cases** cards: compact **Basic case info** / **Evidence** / **Submission draft reviewed** checklist when progress loaded (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî compact readiness checklist on All cases cards**). |
| **Packet generation** | `src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx` ‚Äî aggregate intake, timeline, evidence, filings, tasks for review/export/copy/print; **primary** post‚Äìdraft-review destination from **`/justice/plan`** (`Review prepared next step`). When **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming`** applies (¬ß2), emerald **Your prepared action review** / **Your approved case packet** card + **pre-approval explainer** / **readiness bridge** (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî prepared review explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/packet`)**) + **post-approval approved-step explainer** (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**) + optional approval checkpoint; approved state persists via **`client_state.prepared_packet_approved`** and **`client_state.approved_next_action`** (**`PATCH`** existing case API) for signed-in **UUID** cases plus session fallbacks (¬ß2) ‚Äî **no** new routes/schema/timeline types; **no** auto-submit. Packet hydrates **`approved_next_action.status`** (**`approved`**, **`started`**, or **`completed`**) and shows **Next action started** / **Opened for next step**, **Next action recorded as handled**, or saved **outcome / follow-up** summary when applicable (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî approved next action started surfaced**, **Approved next action completed / handled**, **Approved next action outcome / follow-up tracking**). **`/justice/plan`** and **`/justice/packet`** mark **`started`** on approved **Open {label}** click before navigation (¬ß2 **Approved next action started**, **Packet ‚Äî Open approved step marks started tracking (`/justice/packet`)**); **`/justice/plan`** records **`completed`** when started, saves **outcome / follow-up** when **`completed`**, and surfaces all states after return/refresh (¬ß2). |
| **Submission draft preview** | `src/app/justice/preview/page.tsx` ‚Äî user reviews what would be submitted **before** any filing. **Deterministic** plain text from **`buildSubmissionDraftPreview.ts`** remains **source of truth / fallback**. **Optional AI-assisted** draft: **`POST /api/justice/preview-draft`** (authenticated, rate-limited, **`OPENAI_API_KEY`** server-side only) + **`buildSubmissionDraftAiPrompt.ts`**; bounded JSON body; optional **`case_id`** UUID gated with **`userOwnsJusticeCase`**; AI output **review-only**; UI discloses **OpenAI**. **Proof on your case** card (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî proof on your case card (Chat AI handoff continuity)**): reuses existing **`GET /api/justice/evidence`** via **`loadEvidence`** ‚Äî loading/error/empty/saved states; count + up to **3** recent proof note titles (type/date when available); empty links to **`/justice/chat-ai`**; metadata-only copy; intro clarifies saved chat intake/case and proof titles in draft ‚Äî **no** new API. **Review milestone:** **`submission_draft_reviewed`** timeline event when the user continues to **`/justice/plan`** ‚Äî **`POST /api/justice/submission-draft-reviewed`** for owned UUID cases (returns **`timeline`** for **`applyServerTimelineFromResponse`**), else **`appendSubmissionDraftReviewedOnce`** (session). **`/justice/plan`** (`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`): timeline status summary can read **Submission draft reviewed.**; when the milestone is present and the case has **not** moved past that stage (not merchant-resolved; no prep-opened / complaint-filed / **FTC practice completed** yet), **post-review handoff** shows emerald **Surrenderless prepared your next step** (**`pickPreparedNextAction`**: primary **`Review prepared next step`** ‚Üí **`/justice/packet`**; **next-step explainer** + **readiness bridge** when not ready to escalate ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî post-draft next-step explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/plan`)**; optional secondary **Open {focus} preparation** to an internal prep route; full plan below)‚Äî**UI-only**; **no** new APIs, schema, timeline writes beyond the existing milestone, **`rules.ts`** changes, filing automation, queue workers, or real submission behavior; **no** task auto-creation. **`recommendationText`** remains in the **Recommended next** panel only; destination rows that **already** show **Recommended next** get **accent** styling. |
| **Action routing / rules** | `src/lib/justice/rules.ts` ‚Äî destination ordering, locks, FTC/CFPB/FCC relevance, **DOT/aviation hints** (**`dotLikelyRelevant`**) and **`internalRoute: "/justice/dot"`** when matched (unresolved plans), **`small_claims`** with **`internalRoute: "/justice/demand-letter"`** (**`status: "later"`**; not primary **Step 3**), payment dispute availability. **`/justice/plan`** (**`Other places this may go`**): **BBB**, **State AG**, **CFPB**, **FCC**, **DOT**, and **`small_claims` / demand letter** rows can show a **collapsed** **metadata-only** preview when **`internalRoute`** is set (see ¬ß2). **Step 3** priority on the plan: **CFPB ‚Üí FCC ‚Üí DOT ‚Üí FTC fallback** (see ¬ß2). |
| **Merchant / company contact message** | **`src/lib/justice/buildMerchantContactMessage.ts`** ‚Äî deterministic letter from **`JusticeIntake`**; consumed by **`/justice/merchant`** (full copy-and-save) and **`/justice/plan`** (compact **Suggested message** preview when contact is **recommended** / **`merchantBadge`**). **`/justice/plan`** (`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`) also surfaces a **separate** **Final follow-up before escalation** preview (saved contact metadata + plan-only deterministic copy; **not** **`buildMerchantMessage`**) when contact is saved, **FTC** is unlocked, the case is unresolved, and the first-contact preview is **not** shown ‚Äî **no** change to **`merchantBadge`** / first-contact preview behavior. |
| **Payment dispute bank/card letter** | **`src/lib/justice/buildPaymentDisputeBankLetter.ts`** ‚Äî deterministic issuer letter from checklist draft + **`JusticeIntake`**; consumed by **`/justice/payment-dispute`** (full checklist/copy/save) and **`/justice/plan`** (compact preview when payment dispute is available/recommended). |

New conversational UI should **read and write** these same primitives (intake shape can evolve carefully; prefer additive fields and migrations if the schema changes). **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`** is the shared **forward** assembler (**`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**), **reverse** mapper (**`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**), defaults (**`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**), and contact-proof gate (**`validateContactProofForIntake`**) for **AI** and **scripted** chat intake (structured form can stay aligned via the same parts shape); **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** + **`/justice/chat-ai`** are the **primary** conversational path, including **Update in chat** (¬ß2) and **proof/evidence guidance** that links into **`/justice/evidence`** without auto-creating rows (¬ß2); **`/justice/chat`** and **`/justice/intake`** remain **fallbacks** (¬ß2). Long-term goal (¬ß1): user **only chats**; Surrenderless gathers facts, structures the case, organizes proof, prepares submissions, gets approval, submits/queues where feasible, tracks follow-ups ‚Äî **not** full filing automation yet.

---

## 4. What should not be expanded blindly

- **Do not** keep adding **disconnected form pages** as the primary UX; each new `/justice/*` wizard is debt unless it converges on chat-first or a single shell.
- **Do not** treat **external links + manual filing** as the **final** product story; they are acceptable **transition** paths, not the north star.
- **Do not** grow **mock/demo flows** (e.g. internal practice forms) as if they were **production** regulatory submission; label them, isolate them, and avoid coupling core case state to test-only pages.

---

## 5. Near-term direction

**Bend the Consumer Justice MVP toward chat-first intake and action** while **preserving** persistence and case management:

- **`/justice/chat-ai` is shipped** as the **primary AI conversational intake** and **Update in chat** for the active case (hub/header **Chat intake**; plan **Update in chat**; preview/plan/prep link alignment ¬ß2). **Hydration:** on mount, valid local **`JusticeIntake`** ‚Üí **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** + loaded-case greeting/recap (¬ß2). **Active case banner (UI):** on **Update in chat**, compact **Basic case info** / **Evidence** / **Submission draft reviewed** checklist in **Active case** banner (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**); when **`approvedNextAction`** exists, read-only **Next step: {label}** and **Approved next action: {Approved|Started|Handled}** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî approved next-step label/status on Active case banner (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**) ‚Äî **Open** / **Record handled** stay in Recap **Current action tracking** only. **Current action tracking (UI):** when **`approved_next_action`** exists, **Recap** shows **Current action tracking** ‚Äî next step, status, outcome note, follow-up timing, **Request Surrenderless handling** when **`handling_requested_at`** is missing (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî handling requested in Current action tracking**), **Surrenderless handling requested** after request, **display-only derived queue status** when **`handling_requested_at`** is set on a loaded case (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî display-only derived handling queue status**), read-only handling when **`status === "completed"`** with handling requested (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî read-only handling UI when approved action is handled**), handled-action open-handling triage helper when **`status === "completed"`** with handling requested and unacknowledged (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî handled-action open-handling triage note in Current action tracking**), **View in handling workbench** when handling requested (¬ß2 **Handling workbench ‚Äî active-case back-link from plan and chat-ai**), **Mark acknowledged** when handling requested and not yet acknowledged (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî acknowledge handling request in Current action tracking**), **Open {label}** when **`status === "approved"`** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Open approved step marks started in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**), **Opened for next step.** + **Record action handled for now** when **`status === "started"`** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî record action handled in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**), **Next action recorded as handled for now** (+ step **label** when present) and **Tracking only ‚Äî not automatic filing or submission.** when **`status === "completed"`** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî completed-step clarity in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**), links to **`/justice/plan`** and **`/justice/packet`**; **Mark follow-up handled** when **`follow_up_needed === true`** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî approved next action display hydrate**). **Proof/evidence guidance (UI/copy):** Recap **Proof / evidence** panel + **Organize evidence** ‚Üí **`/justice/evidence`**; optional before preview; metadata-only (notes/links, **no file uploads**); **no** auto-create from chat (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî proof/evidence guidance**). **Saved evidence count** on **Update in chat** when signed in + **UUID** case id (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). **Add a proof note** + **Recent proof notes** (up to **3** rows when **N > 0**, inline **Edit** / **Delete** on displayed rows) via **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** / existing **`GET`** + **`POST`** + **`PATCH`** + **`DELETE`** ‚Äî add form optional **evidence date** / **description**; edit via **`PATCH /api/justice/evidence/[id]`**; delete via **`DELETE /api/justice/evidence/[id]`** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî delete recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); **proof keyword nudge** after successful chat send on **Update in chat** with local **Add a proof note** prefill (empty fields only ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); **fresh-intake staged proof notes** in **`sessionStorage`** via **`stagedProofNotes.ts`**, flushed after confirmed **create** commit; **cross-mode** pending list + flush retry to existing session **UUID** (including **Update in chat** after refresh ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)**). **Continue handoff (UI):** compact **What happens next** panel above **Continue** mirrors save/flush/preview/action-plan paths (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff panel (What happens next)**). **Commit:** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** returns **`{ caseId, serverPersisted }`**; **`mode: "update"`** preserves case id/timeline and **PATCH**es when signed in + UUID; **`mode: "create"`** for brand-new intake (unchanged semantics). **`/justice/chat` is shipped** as the **step-by-step scripted fallback** (unchanged scripted Q&A; always **create** commit). **`/justice/intake`** remains the **structured form fallback** (**Edit structured form**; **create** commit only ‚Äî duplicate-case risk on edit pre-existing). All paths share post-commit **`/justice/preview`** ‚Üí **`/justice/plan`** (¬ß1 north star: chat-first action, **not** auto-filing yet). Company website: **`normalizeCompanyWebsite.ts`** on form + scripted chat.

- **`/justice/chat-ai` session change summary (Update in chat)** is **shipped**: **`chat-ai/page.tsx`** + **`summarizeBuildJusticeIntakePartsSessionChanges.ts`** ‚Äî baseline **`parts`** on hydrate; compares to current **`parts`** in same update session; **Updated in this chat** standalone panel when changes detected and Continue handoff not yet visible; when handoff visible, changes fold into handoff instead (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff session-change integration (Update in chat)**); company/website/what happened/requested outcome/contact details/consumer state; **Added proof note(s) this visit** when saved evidence count safely increases; hidden on fresh intake and no-change sessions; **`handleSend`**, **Continue**, commit, proof CRUD, staged proof, active-case banner, prompts, APIs, schema, hub, cases, plan unchanged ‚Äî **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî session change summary (Update in chat)**).
- **`/justice/plan` FTC practice preview** is **shipped**: inside **Step 3 ‚Äî Escalate to FTC** when that **FTC fallback** Step 3 path is active (not when **CFPB**, **FCC**, or **DOT** is primary Step 3), **FTC is unlocked** and **mock practice is not yet completed**, a **collapsed** preview shows **metadata only** from **`JusticeIntake`** (company, category, optional money/date/email, truncated story) plus **practice-only** disclaimers (**not** a real FTC filing; **no** automatic government submission; **no** external FTC site). Users continue via **`/justice/ftc-review`** for the **full** internal practice form and autofill; **`/mock/ftc-complaint`** stays **internal QA** only. **No** **`submit-form`** / API / timeline changes from the preview, **no** automatic filings/evidence/tasks, **no** filing automation or embedded browser, **no** schema or new tables; **merchant**, **payment**, **evidence**, and **filing** plan previews unchanged.
- **`/justice/plan` BBB / State AG / CFPB / FCC / DOT / demand letter (`small_claims`) destination previews** are **shipped**: in **Other places this may go**, **BBB**, **State AG**, **CFPB**, **FCC**, **USDOT / aviation**, and **Small claims / demand letter** (**`small_claims`**) rows with **`internalRoute`** show a **collapsed** **metadata-only** block (company, category, optional money/date, optional state for AG only, merchant contact summary, truncated story) **before/near** the existing **Open** control ‚Äî **no** full draft on the plan; guidance points users to copy the full draft on **`/justice/bbb`**, **`/justice/state-ag`**, **`/justice/cfpb`**, **`/justice/fcc`**, **`/justice/dot`**, or **`/justice/demand-letter`**; **manual prep**, **Surrenderless does not file** automatically. **`small_claims`** stays **`status: "later"`** and is **not** primary **Step 3**. **Ordering**, badges, **`Open`** links, and **`bbb_prep_opened` / `state_ag_prep_opened` / `cfpb_prep_opened` / `fcc_prep_opened` / `dot_prep_opened` / `demand_letter_prep_opened`** analytics follow the shipped pattern; **DOT** adds **`internalRoute`** when aviation hints match; **`small_claims`** uses **`internalRoute: "/justice/demand-letter"`**. **No** new backend APIs for this slice, **no** tasks, **no** automatic filings/evidence, **no** new timeline **types** from prep-open alone, **no** filing automation, **no** embedded browser, **no** schema or new tables, **no** preview-review tracking changes beyond this routing; **merchant**, **payment**, **evidence**, **filing**, **FTC** (fallback Step 3), and **final follow-up** previews **unchanged** except **DOT** may be **primary Step 3** when relevant (see ¬ß2).
- **`/justice/demand-letter` manual demand-letter prep** is **shipped**: neutral copy-ready letter text, case summary, company/person, story, requested resolution, evidence checklist, saved evidence list, user-driven filing records; **not** legal advice; **no** small-claims eligibility determination; **no** filing, court submission, embedded court browser, or automation; users directed to verify rules with **official / local court** resources; **no** schema/DB/task/auto-filing/auto-evidence changes (see ¬ß2).
- **`/justice/dot` USDOT / aviation manual prep** is **shipped**: copy-ready aviation complaint text, evidence checklist, saved evidence list, user-driven filing records; **no** automatic filing, **no** embedded DOT site, **no** government submission from the app, **no** new APIs, **no** schema/DB/task/auto-evidence changes. **`/justice/plan`** Step 3 priority: **CFPB ‚Üí FCC ‚Üí DOT ‚Üí FTC fallback** (see ¬ß2).
- **`/justice` Consumer Justice workspace hub** is **shipped**: thin landing at **`src/app/justice/page.tsx`** with intro copy (organize issues into an action plan; drafts/checklists/records; **no** automatic filing); **recommended: start with chat intake** (AI conversational **`/justice/chat-ai`**); form intake available for users who prefer the structured form; link cards **Start with chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) first, **Use step-by-step chat** (**`/justice/chat`**; ¬ß2), then plan, form intake, saved cases; optional **session-only Current case** block (**`JusticeHubWorkspaceBody`**) when local intake exists (see ¬ß2); **Current case** client refresh on **visible tab**, **window focus**, and **`storage`** (see ¬ß2); **Needs more info** **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** on **Current case** when basics or saved proof are missing (¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**); static **Continue current action plan** card hidden then; also the **recovery hub** when resume/hydration fails ‚Äî **`router.replace("/justice")`** / **`router.push("/justice")`** instead of **`/justice/intake`** (see ¬ß2 **Justice workspace recovery routing**). **Header** **Justice** ‚Üí **Chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) ‚Üí **Consumer case** (see ¬ß2). Hub/header ordering is **UI only** ‚Äî **no** case-list **`GET`** from the hub, **no** plan logic duplicate, **no** new APIs/schema/auth/persistence/LLM/prompt/parser/builder/commit/preview/plan/**`rules.ts`**/readiness changes beyond **read-only** session reads plus active-case evidence count for chat routing (¬ß2). **Intake finish:** **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** route to **`/justice/preview`** after commit (**`create`** or chat-ai **`update`**; ¬ß2). **`/justice/plan`** remains the full action plan.
- **Next (workspace):** evolve beyond the thin **`/justice`** hub toward a richer shell with **case status**, **next actions**, and **approval previews** without scattering state across many routes ‚Äî the hub is a **start**, not the final chat-first workspace.
- Reuse **timeline + tasks + filings** for ‚Äúwhat happened / what‚Äôs next‚Äù instead of duplicating status in ad-hoc UI only.
- Keep **server timeline append** and **PATCH case** patterns for anything that must stay consistent under automation later.
- **Next:** extend **LLM-assisted** follow-ups and in-app action (fewer manual forms/tabs/external links; more guided steps inside the app) while keeping the same persistence primitives; avoid parallel ad-hoc state outside `JusticeIntake` + session keys. **Shipped:** hydrate **`/justice/chat-ai`** + **update** commit (¬ß2); chat-ai **proof/evidence guidance** (¬ß2); chat-ai **saved evidence count** in Recap via **`GET /api/justice/evidence`** (¬ß2); chat-ai **Add a proof note** on **Update in chat** via existing **`POST /api/justice/evidence`** with optional **evidence date** / **description** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); chat-ai **Recent proof notes** when **N > 0** with inline **Edit** via **`PATCH /api/justice/evidence/[id]`** and **Delete** via **`DELETE /api/justice/evidence/[id]`** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî delete recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); chat-ai **client-side proof keyword nudge** after successful send with local **Add a proof note** prefill (empty fields only ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); chat-ai **fresh-intake staged proof notes** via **`stagedProofNotes.ts`**, flush after confirmed **create** with **cross-mode** pending visibility + retry flush to session **UUID** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)**); chat-ai **Continue handoff** **What happens next** panel (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff panel (What happens next)**); **preview proof on your case** card continuing Chat AI handoff (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî proof on your case card (Chat AI handoff continuity)**); **plan proof readiness continuity** after preview review (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî proof readiness continuity after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**); **plan Case readiness checklist proof CTA** on **Evidence added** when no proof (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist proof CTA (`/justice/plan`)**); **plan Case readiness checklist basics CTA** on **Basic case info present** when basics incomplete (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist basics CTA (`/justice/plan`)**); **plan Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA** (**Submission draft reviewed: yes/not yet**, **Review submission draft** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** when not reviewed ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA (`/justice/plan`)**); **plan post-draft chat continuity prompt** with **Update in chat** after action plan shown (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî post-draft chat continuity prompt after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**); **plan post-draft re-preview continuity prompt** with **Review submission draft again** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** after chat updates (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî post-draft re-preview continuity prompt after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**); **plan post-draft next-step explainer and readiness bridge** (**`getPreparedNextStepExplainer`**, no auto-file/submit copy, **Before you escalate, finish readiness:** chat/preview links when **`!readyToEscalate`**; **Review prepared next step** CTA unchanged ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî post-draft next-step explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/plan`)**); **packet prepared review explainer and readiness bridge** on **`/justice/packet`** pre-approval card (**`getPreparedPacketReviewExplainer`**, **`stepLabel`**, **Before you approve, finish readiness:**, **Update in chat** correction ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî prepared review explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/packet`)**); **packet post-approval approved-step explainer** on **`/justice/packet`** after approval (**`getApprovedPacketNextStepExplainer`**, **Your approved case packet**, **Open {label}** in-app prep/tracking clarity ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**); **saved cases Needs more info chat routing** (**Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** on **All cases** cards ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**); **saved cases compact readiness checklist** on each **All cases** card when progress loaded (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî compact readiness checklist on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**); **hub Current case Needs more info chat routing** (¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**); **hub Current case compact readiness checklist** (basics/evidence/draft yes-not-yet + inline chat/preview links ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Justice hub ‚Äî Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**); **chat-ai active case compact readiness checklist** on **Update in chat** **Active case** banner (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**); **chat-ai active case context banner** when **Update in chat** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî active case context banner (Update in chat)**); **chat-ai session change summary** on **Update in chat** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî session change summary (Update in chat)**); **chat-ai Continue handoff session-change integration** (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff session-change integration (Update in chat)**); **preview chat-update continuity card** after **Update in chat** Continue (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî chat-update continuity card (Chat AI handoff)**); **preview pre-plan chat correction prompt** (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî pre-plan chat correction prompt (`/justice/preview`)**). **Still to do:** richer in-chat proof (**LLM/system-prompt** proof nudges in **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** ‚Äî separate from client keyword nudge ¬ß2; fresh-intake keyword nudge; staged proof edit/delete); structured-form safe update on submit; timeline ‚Äúintake updated‚Äù milestone if needed; filing queue and follow-up tracking (¬ß1) ‚Äî **without** expanding auto-filing until product-ready.

## 6. Current technical map

### Major app routes (`src/app/**/page.tsx`)

| Area | Paths (representative) |
|------|-------------------------|
| Legacy / misc | `/` (home), `/dashboard`, `/admin`, `/sign-in`, `/debug/me` |
| Justice | **`/justice`** (thin Consumer Justice **workspace hub** ‚Äî **recommends AI chat intake**; **Current case** re-read from local session/timeline helpers on **tab visible**, **window focus**, **`storage`** (¬ß2); **recovery hub** when resume/hydration fails (**`router.replace("/justice")`** / **`router.push("/justice")`** fallback; ¬ß2 **Justice workspace recovery routing**); form intake for structured form; optional **session-only** **Current case** card + **conditional** hub links via **`JusticeHubWorkspaceBody`** when valid local intake: static **Continue current action plan** card **hidden**; link cards **chat first** (**Start with chat intake** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **Use step-by-step chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat`**; ¬ß2), then plan or intake/cases; explains organize ‚Üí action plan, drafts/checklists/records, **no** automatic filing; **no** server case **`GET`** on hub, **no** plan duplicate; hub/header ordering **UI-only**), **`/justice/intake`** (form intake ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** ‚Üí plan; **create** commit only), **`/justice/chat-ai`** (primary **AI conversational** intake + **Update in chat**; mount hydrate via **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake`** + **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**; Recap **Proof / evidence** guidance + **Organize evidence** ‚Üí **`/justice/evidence`**; **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`**; **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **`create`** or **`update`**; evidence **not** required before preview; ¬ß2), **`/justice/chat`** (scripted step-by-step chat intake; **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** + **`validateContactProofForIntake`** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** ‚Üí plan; **unchanged** scripted Q&A; **create** commit; ¬ß2), **`/justice/plan`** (readiness + recommendations; breadcrumb **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`** (hydrate/update), **Edit structured form** ‚Üí **`/justice/intake`**; signed-out **Start a new case** ‚Üí **`/justice`**; ¬ß2; existing **`GET /api/justice/cases/[id]`** / list hydrate reads **`client_state.prepared_packet_approved`** + session fallback; when approved after packet, **Prepared packet approved for next action** callout + **View approved case packet** / **View case packet** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî prepared packet approval surfaced**; after **`submission_draft_reviewed`**, when user has not moved on: **Submission draft reviewed** + optional **Surrenderless prepared your next step** (**`pickPreparedNextAction`**: primary **`Review prepared next step`** ‚Üí **`/justice/packet`**, **not filed automatically** copy; full plan below ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî prepared next action**; **UI-only**, **no** new APIs/schema/timeline writes beyond existing milestone); **`recommendationText`** in **Recommended next** panel; **accent** on rows **already** **Recommended next**; **compact Suggested message** preview for merchant/company contact when **recommended**, same helper as **`/justice/merchant`**; **separate Final follow-up before escalation** preview on the same card when contact is saved, **FTC** unlocked, unresolved, and first-contact preview not shown ‚Äî plan-only deterministic copy + saved-contact summary, link **`/justice/merchant`**; **compact Suggested bank/card dispute letter** preview when payment dispute is **available/recommended**, same helper as **`/justice/payment-dispute`**; **saved evidence metadata** preview under Evidence / proof when signed in and rows exist, same **`GET /api/justice/evidence`** as readiness; **saved filing metadata** preview under Filing records when signed in and rows exist, same **`GET /api/justice/filings`** as readiness; **Step 3** escalation priority **CFPB ‚Üí FCC ‚Üí DOT ‚Üí FTC fallback**; **FTC practice preview** inside **Step 3 ‚Äî Escalate to FTC** when that **fallback** path is active, **FTC** is unlocked and mock practice is not yet completed ‚Äî **metadata-only** from **`JusticeIntake`**, collapsed/truncated UI, practice-only copy, link to **`/justice/ftc-review`** for full internal practice; **primary Step 3 ‚Äî Escalate to DOT** with CTA to **`/justice/dot`** when aviation hints match and CFPB/FCC are not primary; **Other places this may go**: **collapsed metadata-only** previews on **BBB**, **State AG**, **CFPB**, **FCC**, **DOT**, and **Small claims / demand letter** (**`small_claims`**) rows when **`internalRoute`** is set ‚Äî manual prep copy, truncated story, **no** full draft on plan; **`small_claims`** stays **later** (not primary Step 3); **Open** links include **`/justice/bbb`**, **`/justice/state-ag`**, **`/justice/cfpb`**, **`/justice/fcc`**, **`/justice/dot`**, **`/justice/demand-letter`**), **`/justice/preview`** (deterministic + optional AI-assisted submission draft preview; no-case **Chat intake** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **Step-by-step chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat`**, **Structured form** ‚Üí **`/justice/intake`**; ¬ß2 **Justice-wide navigation alignment**), **`/justice/merchant`** (full deterministic contact message + copy + save contact/proof), **`/justice/payment-dispute`** (full payment dispute checklist + copy + save **`payment_dispute_draft`** / timeline), **`/justice/ftc-review`** (full internal FTC practice review + optional autofill; not a real government filing), **`/justice/bbb`** (BBB complaint prep + copy-ready draft; manual filing), **`/justice/state-ag`** (State AG complaint prep + copy-ready draft; manual filing), **`/justice/cfpb`** (CFPB complaint prep + copy-ready draft; manual filing), **`/justice/fcc`** (FCC complaint prep + copy-ready draft; manual filing), **`/justice/dot`** (USDOT / aviation consumer complaint prep + copy-ready draft + checklist + saved evidence + user-driven filing records; manual filing only; **no** embed, **no** auto-submit), **`/justice/demand-letter`** (manual demand-letter prep from **`JusticeIntake`**; not legal advice; **no** small-claims eligibility determination; **no** court filing or embed; copy-ready letter + checklist + saved evidence + user-driven filing records), **`/justice/evidence`** (full evidence add/edit/delete), `/justice/cases` (**Start new case** ‚Üí **`/justice`** after **`clearLocalJusticeSession`**; **Needs attention** + conditional **readiness helper** when not ready; ¬ß2), `/justice/cases/archived`, **`/justice/packet`** (packet export + **`JusticeFilingRecords`** filing CRUD) |
| Internal QA | `/mock/ftc-complaint` |

### Major Justice components (`src/app/components/`)

- **`Header.tsx`** ‚Äî Global nav links (order): **Justice** (`/justice` workspace hub), **Chat intake** (`/justice/chat-ai`), **Consumer case** (`/justice/intake` structured form), plus Clerk controls; used across Justice pages. Promotes **AI chat-first** entry (¬ß2 hub/header + ¬ß2 **Justice-wide navigation alignment** on preview/plan/prep); scripted **`/justice/chat`** **Q&A** unchanged; all intake paths route to **`/justice/preview`** after commit (**chat-ai** **`update`** when case hydrated; ¬ß2).
- **`JusticeActionResumeSignInPrompt.tsx`** ‚Äî Hydration gate when session/user is insufficient; **Start new case** routing targets **`/justice`** workspace (chat-first hub) where aligned with ¬ß2 recovery routing.
- **`JusticeSavedEvidenceList.tsx`** ‚Äî Evidence list for current session case (prep pages).
- **`JusticeFilingRecords.tsx`** ‚Äî Filing CRUD for current case.
- **`JusticeCaseTasks.tsx`** ‚Äî Task CRUD + due badges; used on **plan** and **packet** (not every prep page).

### Justice API routes (`src/app/api/justice/`)

- **`cases`** ‚Äî `GET` list (non-archived default; `?archived=1` for archived); optional **`limit`** (default **10**, max **50**) and **`offset`** pagination; JSON **`{ cases, has_more, offset, limit }`**; `POST` create.
- **`cases/[id]`** ‚Äî `GET` one case; `PATCH` intake, timeline, drafts, `archived_at`, `case_label`.
- **`evidence`**, **`evidence/[id]`** ‚Äî List/create; update/delete; POST may append server timeline (`evidence_added`).
- **`filings`**, **`filings/[id]`** ‚Äî Same pattern; `filing_recorded` on create.
- **`tasks`**, **`tasks/[id]`** ‚Äî Same pattern; `task_added` / completion-related updates.
- **`events`** ‚Äî Authenticated analytics append (expects a `history`-style table in Supabase; **not defined in repo migrations** ‚Äî see limitations).
- **`preview-draft`** ‚Äî `POST` only: optional **AI-assisted** plain-text submission draft for **`/justice/preview`**. **Clerk** (`getUserOr401`), **`rateLimit`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY`** server-side; validates intake + destination + bounded evidence/timeline; optional **`case_id`** with **`userOwnsJusticeCase`**; returns `{ draft }` JSON; **no** persistence or filing.
- **`intake-chat`** ‚Äî `POST` only: **endpoint-only** AI conversational intake turn (¬ß2). **Clerk** (`getUserOr401`), **`rateLimit`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY`** server-side; body **`{ user_message, parts, conversation_history? }`**; returns **`{ assistantMessage, parts }`** (`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`); **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** + **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`**; **no** DB, timeline, case creation, or commit.
- **`submission-draft-reviewed`** ‚Äî `POST` only: records **`submission_draft_reviewed`** on **`justice_cases.timeline`** (idempotent **`appendCaseTimelineEntry`**). **Clerk** (`getUserOr401`), UUID **`case_id`**, **`userOwnsJusticeCase`**; optional **`destination_label`** / **`used_ai`** for entry **detail**; returns **`{ timeline }`** for client merge (**`applyServerTimelineFromResponse`**). **No** filing records, tasks, or schema changes ‚Äî **tracking only**.

### Supabase tables (from `supabase/migrations/`)

| Table | Purpose |
|-------|---------|
| **`justice_cases`** | `id`, `user_id` (text), `intake` (jsonb), `timeline` (jsonb), `payment_dispute_draft`, `client_state`, timestamps, `archived_at`, `case_label`. RLS enabled; **no policies on cases** ‚Äî access enforced in API with Clerk `user_id` + admin client. |
| **`justice_case_evidence`** | Metadata evidence rows; optional `source_url`, `storage_note`. RLS policies use **`authenticated` / `auth.uid()`** ‚Äî **not** how server routes access data (service role bypasses RLS). |
| **`justice_case_filings`** | Manual/external filing records. |
| **`justice_case_tasks`** | Follow-up tasks. |

**Referenced in code but not in repo migrations:** `users` (profile init upsert), `history` (justice events). Deployments must define these separately or migrations must be added.

### Key libraries (`src/lib/justice/`)

- **`types.ts`** ‚Äî `JusticeIntake`, timeline types (including **`submission_draft_reviewed`**), **`JusticeApprovedNextAction`** (`label`, `href`, **`status: "approved" | "started"`**, `approved_at`, `started_at`) and **`JusticeCaseClientState`** (`prepared_packet_approved`, **`approved_next_action`** on **`justice_cases.client_state`**), **storage key constants**.
- **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer.ts`** ‚Äî Shared client helper used by **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`**. **`mode: "create"`** (default): new **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, **`clearTimelineForNewCase`**, **`case_started`**, clears FTC/mock keys, **`POST /api/justice/cases`** when signed in (session fallback on failure), server id/timeline merge, **`intake_completed`** analytics. **`mode: "update"`** (**`/justice/chat-ai`** when case hydrated): preserves **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** and timeline, writes **`STORAGE_INTAKE`**, **`PATCH /api/justice/cases/[id]`** when signed in + UUID (no **`POST`**, no **`case_started`**, no FTC clears, no **`intake_completed`**). Callers **`router.push("/justice/preview")`** then **`/justice/plan`** after preview continue.
- **`normalizeCompanyWebsite.ts`** ‚Äî Shared normalizer for **`company_website`** on **`/justice/intake`** and **`/justice/chat`**: empty / `none` / `n/a` / `-` / `no` ‚Üí `""`; values already starting with **`http://`** or **`https://`** unchanged; bare hosts (e.g. **`amazon.com`**) ‚Üí **`https://amazon.com`**. Form intake uses **`type="text"`** (not **`type="url"`**) so bare domains are not blocked by the browser.
- **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`** ‚Äî Shared **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** module: **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**, forward **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** (trims, **`normalizeCompanyWebsite`**, merges money + desired outcome into **`money_involved`**, conditional contact fields, **`consumer_us_state`**), reverse **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (hydrate **`JusticeIntake`** for chat-ai/plan **Update in chat**), and **`validateContactProofForIntake`**. Used by **`/justice/chat`** and **`/justice/chat-ai`** before **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** (**`create`** or **`update`**) ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** ‚Üí **`/justice/plan`** (¬ß2).
- **`timeline.ts`** ‚Äî Session timeline store, sync helpers, many `append*Once` helpers, **`appendSubmissionDraftReviewedOnce`** / **`buildSubmissionDraftReviewedDetail`** / stable id for preview‚Üíplan review milestone.
- **`rules.ts`** ‚Äî Destination computation and gating; **CFPB**, **FCC**, and **DOT/aviation** relevance (**`dotLikelyRelevant`**); **`internalRoute: "/justice/dot"`** when DOT hints match (unresolved plans); **`small_claims`** with **`internalRoute: "/justice/demand-letter"`** (**`status: "later"`**; not primary **Step 3**); FTC unlock and payment dispute availability.
- **`buildSubmissionDraftPreview.ts`** ‚Äî Pure, deterministic plain-text draft for **`/justice/preview`** from **`JusticeIntake`**, selected destination label/id, and optional evidence titles (**source of truth**; no external AI).
- **`buildSubmissionDraftAiPrompt.ts`** ‚Äî Pure system/user message builder for **`POST /api/justice/preview-draft`** (constraints: not legal advice, not filed, faithful to facts, plain text, no fake URLs); consumed only on the server.
- **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** ‚Äî Pure message builder for **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`**; model returns JSON **`{ assistantMessage, parts }`** aligned with **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`**; explicit rules to fill **`purchase_or_signup`** when the complained-about object is clearly stated (¬ß2 **AI intake ‚Äî `purchase_or_signup` extraction**).
- **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`** ‚Äî Request **`parts`** clamp/coerce, optional **`conversation_history`** cap, merge/parse model JSON before API response; imports **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** from **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (re-exported for **`/justice/chat-ai`**); consumed only by **`intake-chat`** route. **Contract unchanged.**
- **`buildMerchantContactMessage.ts`** ‚Äî Pure deterministic merchant/company contact letter from **`JusticeIntake`** (**`buildMerchantMessage`**, **`cfpbFinancialProductSummary`**); used by **`/justice/merchant`** and the **`/justice/plan`** compact preview (no sending, no new persistence from the preview alone).
- **`buildPaymentDisputeBankLetter.ts`** ‚Äî Pure deterministic bank/card issuer dispute letter from checklist draft + **`JusticeIntake`** (**`buildBankLetter`**, **`buildDefaultPaymentDisputeDraft`**); used by **`/justice/payment-dispute`** and the **`/justice/plan`** compact preview (no sending automation, no new persistence from the preview alone).
- **`caseReadiness.ts`**, **`caseApiValidation.ts`**, **`hydrateActiveCaseFromServer.ts`**, **`clearLocalJusticeSession.ts`**, **`taskDueStatus.ts`**, **`useJusticeActionPageHydration.ts`** (**signed-in** resume-from-list failure ‚Üí **`/justice`**; see ¬ß2 **Justice workspace recovery routing**), etc.

### Session / local storage keys (from `src/lib/justice/types.ts` and `clearLocalJusticeSession.ts`)

| Key constant | Storage key string | Purpose |
|--------------|-------------------|---------|
| `STORAGE_INTAKE` | `justice_intake_v1` | Active case intake JSON |
| `STORAGE_CASE_ID` | `justice_case_id` | Active case UUID |
| `STORAGE_TIMELINE_V1` | `justice_timeline_v1` | JSON map of case id ‚Üí timeline entries |
| `STORAGE_PAYMENT_DISPUTE_CHECKLIST_DRAFT_V1` | `justice_payment_dispute_checklist_draft_v1` | Payment dispute draft |
| `STORAGE_FTC_MANUAL_UNLOCK` | `justice_ftc_manual_unlock` | Manual FTC unlock flag |
| (session) | `justice_ftc_mock_completed` | Mock FTC lane completion (cleared with full justice session clear) |

### Auth / server

- **Clerk:** `ClerkProvider` in `src/app/layout.tsx` and `src/app/providers.tsx` (duplicate provider wrap ‚Äî known quirk).
- **Middleware:** `src/middleware.ts` ‚Äî `clerkMiddleware`; optional `DEPLOY_PASSWORD` Basic Auth gate.
- **API auth:** `src/server/requireUser.ts` ‚Äî `getAuth(request).userId` for Justice routes.

### Known limitations (non-exhaustive)

- **Large saved-case lists:** `GET /api/justice/cases` paginates (**`limit`** / **`offset`**, **`has_more`**); **`/justice/cases`** offers **Load more cases**. Very large offsets or huge histories can still be slow ‚Äî prefer reasonable page sizes.
- **Dual timeline:** Session + DB can drift if sync fails or multiple tabs are used.
- **Pre-server case id:** Intake can generate a non-UUID id in edge environments; evidence/task APIs require UUID `case_id`. **`/justice/chat-ai` update commit** only **PATCH**es the server when the active id is already a UUID; local-only ids still get **`STORAGE_INTAKE`** updated.
- **Structured form edit:** **`/justice/intake`** submit still always uses **create** commit ‚Äî editing a loaded case via the form can still duplicate cases (chat-ai **update** path does not apply there yet).
- **Chat-ai evidence:** On **Update in chat**, **`/justice/chat-ai`** reads **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** via **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** for a **saved evidence count** in Recap (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**), a collapsed **Recent proof notes** block when **N > 0** (up to **3** rows ‚Äî optional date/truncated description; per-row **Edit** / **Delete** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî delete recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**), can **`POST`** via **Add a proof note** (required **title** + **evidence_type**; optional **evidence date** / **description** when trimmed non-empty ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**), can **`PATCH`** displayed recent rows (**title**, **evidence_type**, **`evidence_date`**/**`description`** including **`null`** clear ‚Äî **no** **`source_url`**/**`storage_note`**; **no** **`applyServerTimelineFromResponse`** on edit), and can **`DELETE`** displayed recent rows (**confirm** dialog ‚Äî **no** timeline append; **no** **`source_url`**/**`storage_note`**); **fresh intake** before first server commit can **stage** proof-note metadata locally (**`stagedProofNotes.ts`**, **`canStageProofNoteInChat`**) ‚Äî **pending** count/list whenever staged rows exist (including after **Update in chat** hydrate); first pass flushes via existing **`POST /api/justice/evidence`** after **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** confirms **`serverPersisted`**, or **cross-mode retry-flushes** to session **UUID** when intake + **UUID** case already exist (**no** duplicate **create** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)**); pending/local until **Continue** saves to case; does not show saved count, recent preview, add-to-server, edit, delete, or keyword nudge until **Update in chat** with server-backed case. After successful chat send on **Update in chat**, **client-side proof keyword nudge** may show a dismissible banner toward **Add a proof note** and **prefill empty** title/description from the triggering message (opens **`<details>`** for review; user must still **Save proof note** ‚Äî ¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). **`/justice/evidence`** remains the full list/edit/delete surface (and **`source_url`** / **`storage_note`**). Proof in chat has **metadata capture** on **Update in chat**, **fresh staging** before first server case, **keyword nudge**, and **local prefill** on **Update in chat**; **no** LLM/system-prompt proof capture, **no** auto-created evidence rows, **no** file uploads; staged/saved proof requires user action ‚Äî not AI-inferred.
- **Chat-ai Continue handoff:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** **Recap** shows **What happens next** panel above **Continue to submission preview** when basics complete (**`getPreviewBasicsMissing`**) and **`validateContactProofForIntake`** passes ‚Äî **`getContinueHandoffSteps`** lists steps matching **`handleContinueToPreview`** (save case/updates, pending proof flush where applicable, submission draft preview, action plan from preview); on **Update in chat** with **`sessionChangeLines`**, handoff includes **Save your updates from this chat to your case:** plus each detected change step (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff session-change integration (Update in chat)**); **Continue** disabled while **`submitting`**, **`loading`**, or basics missing; replaces prior staged-proof one-liner above **Continue**; amber **Still needed before preview** and contact-proof warnings unchanged; **no** preview/plan/API/schema/prompt changes (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff panel (What happens next)**).
- **Preview proof continuity:** **`/justice/preview`** shows **Proof on your case** card after **Related action** using existing **`loadEvidence`** / **`GET /api/justice/evidence`** ‚Äî loading (**Loading saved proof notes...**), error (inside card; draft still shown), empty (**Add proof in chat ‚Üí** **`/justice/chat-ai`**), or saved count + up to **3** recent titles with type/date; intro copy clarifies saved chat intake/case and metadata-only proof titles in draft; replaces standalone evidence loading/error lines; **no** new API, draft-builder, plan, schema, or prompt changes (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî proof on your case card (Chat AI handoff continuity)**).
- **Preview chat-update continuity:** **`/justice/preview`** after intake hydration reads **`justice_preview_chat_update_summary_v1`** via **`readAndClearPreviewChatUpdateSummary`** (one-time); **From your chat update** card when valid **`sessionChangeLines`** from **Update in chat** Continue ‚Äî company line, change bullets, draft reflects saved case / nothing filed automatically, **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`**; not on fresh intake, plan ‚Üí preview, or no-change updates; **`previewChatUpdateHandoff.ts`** + chat-ai **`writePreviewChatUpdateSummary`** / **`clearPreviewChatUpdateSummary`** ‚Äî **no** draft generation, review milestone, evidence GET, AI draft, continue-to-plan, commit, hub/cases/plan changes; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî chat-update continuity card (Chat AI handoff)**).
- **Preview pre-plan chat correction:** **`/justice/preview`** bottom review card shows **Need to fix something in the draft?** **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`** and subline to describe changes in chat then return to review updated draft (nothing filed automatically); always when intake loaded, before **Continue to action plan**; **`handleContinueToPlan`**, review checkbox, draft generation, evidence GET, AI draft, chat-update handoff unchanged ‚Äî **no** API, schema, helper, hub, cases, plan, chat-ai changes; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Preview ‚Äî pre-plan chat correction prompt (`/justice/preview`)**).
- **Plan proof readiness continuity:** **`/justice/plan`** post-draft **`showPostDraftReviewCallout`** includes proof line from existing **`evidenceCount`** (**Loading saved proof notes...**, saved count + reviewed-draft metadata wording, or empty + **Add proof in chat**); **Evidence / proof** empty state links **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Add evidence** unchanged; **`evidenceReady`** / escalation logic unchanged; **no** new API, chat-ai, preview, lib, schema, or prompt changes (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî proof readiness continuity after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**).
- **Plan Case readiness checklist proof CTA:** **`/justice/plan`** **Case readiness** **Evidence added** row includes inline **Add proof in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`** when signed in, readiness loaded, and no evidence; mirrors basics CTA link styling; **`evidenceReady`** / **`readyToEscalate`** / **`basicsReady`** / readiness fetch / packet CTAs / post-draft callout / breadcrumb unchanged; **no** API, schema, helper, preview, chat-ai, hub, or cases changes; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist proof CTA (`/justice/plan`)**).
- **Plan Case readiness checklist basics CTA:** **`/justice/plan`** **Case readiness** **Basic case info present** row includes inline **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`** when signed in, readiness loaded, and basics incomplete; mirrors proof CTA pattern; evidence row / draft-review row / breadcrumb / **`basicsReady`** / **`readyToEscalate`** / readiness fetch / packet CTAs / post-draft callout unchanged; **no** API, schema, helper, preview, chat-ai, hub, or cases changes; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist basics CTA (`/justice/plan`)**).
- **Plan Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA:** **`/justice/plan`** **Case readiness** **Submission draft reviewed: yes/not yet** from **`submission_draft_reviewed`** timeline; **Review submission draft** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`** when signed in, readiness loaded, not reviewed; **`basicsReady`** / **`evidenceReady`** / **`readyToEscalate`** / readiness fetch / packet CTAs / post-draft callout / basics/evidence rows / breadcrumb unchanged; **no** API, schema, helper, preview, chat-ai, hub, or cases changes; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA (`/justice/plan`)**).
- **Plan post-draft chat continuity:** **`/justice/plan`** **`showPostDraftReviewCallout`** includes chat-first line after next-step explainer / readiness bridge and proof-readiness and before packet CTA ‚Äî **Update in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`** for fixing details or adding proof notes; **`recommendationText`** / **`pickPreparedNextAction`** / packet approval / handling / evidence logic unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims; **no** new API, chat-ai, preview, packet, lib, schema, or prompt changes (¬ß2 **Plan ‚Äî post-draft chat continuity prompt after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**).

- **Saved cases Needs more info chat routing:** **`/justice/cases`** **All cases** cards in **Needs more info** show **Update in chat** (missing basics) or **Add proof in chat** (basics OK, no evidence) under **`caseReadinessHint`**; **`openUpdateInChat`** runs **`activateCaseInSession`** then **`/justice/chat-ai`**; evidence-only hint mentions chat + evidence page; **`Open case`** ‚Üí **`/justice/plan`** unchanged; compact checklist / readiness predicates/filters/attention unchanged on this slice; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims; **no** new API, hub, plan, chat-ai, **`caseReadiness.ts`**, schema, or prompt changes (¬ß2 **Saved cases ‚Äî Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**).

- **Chat-ai session change summary:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** on **Update in chat** captures hydrated baseline **`parts`** in **`sessionBaselinePartsRef`** (not reset per message) and first **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** count in **`sessionBaselineEvidenceCountRef`**; **`summarizeBuildJusticeIntakePartsSessionChanges`** diffs baseline vs current **`parts`**; **Updated in this chat** standalone panel when changes exist and **What happens next** is not shown; when handoff visible, same lines fold into **`getContinueHandoffSteps`** and standalone panel hidden (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Continue handoff session-change integration (Update in chat)**); hidden on fresh intake / no changes ‚Äî **no** API, schema, timeline, prompts, **`handleSend`**, **Continue**, commit, proof CRUD, staged proof, active-case banner, hub, cases, plan changes; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî session change summary (Update in chat)**).
- **Prepared next action on plan / packet:** Plan **`pickPreparedNextAction`** routes primary CTA to **`/justice/packet`**; packet **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming`** shows prepared-review + **pre-approval explainer** / **readiness bridge** (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî prepared review explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/packet`)**) + **post-approval approved-step explainer** after **`packetApproved`** (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**) + approval UI only when the same post-review gates apply. Packet approval persists in **`client_state`** (**`prepared_packet_approved`** + **`approved_next_action`** with stored **label/href**) for signed-in **UUID** cases (plus session fallbacks). On **`/justice/plan`**, **`/justice/packet`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`**, approved **Open {label}** marks **`approved_next_action.status: "started"`** before navigation (¬ß2 **Approved next action started**, **Packet ‚Äî Open approved step marks started tracking (`/justice/packet`)**, **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Open approved step marks started in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**); **`/justice/packet`** hydrates and displays **started** in the approval area (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî approved next action started surfaced**). Hydrate on both surfaces merges server + session without downgrading **started** (¬ß2 **Approved next action started**). **Not** written to **`timeline`**. Users still **manually** prep, copy, and file externally ‚Äî **no** auto-submit, queue, filing workers, or implication that Surrenderless filed/submitted/sent/contacted anyone (¬ß2).
- **Packet Open approved step started tracking:** **`/justice/packet`** **`handleApprovedNextActionOpen`** on **Open {label}** when **`status === "approved"`** ‚Äî **`started`** + **`started_at`** to session + signed-in **UUID** **`client_state`**, then navigate; mirrors plan; already **`started`**/**`completed`** uses plain **`Link`** without downgrade; approval checkpoint, **`handleApprovePreparedPacket`**, explainer copy, gates, packet body, prep routes, APIs, schema, plan, preview, chat-ai, hub, cases unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî Open approved step marks started tracking (`/justice/packet`)**).
- **Chat-ai Open approved step in Current action tracking:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** **Update in chat** **Recap ‚Üí Current action tracking** when **`status === "approved"`** shows **Open {label}**; **`handleApprovedNextActionOpen`** marks **`started`** + **`started_at`**, updates session **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`**, signed-in **UUID** **`GET` + merge + `PATCH`** **`client_state`**, then navigates to **`href`** ‚Äî completes approved‚Üístarted loop in chat without Plan/Packet; **`started`**/**`completed`** branches unchanged; proof, handling, follow-up, banner, outcome form unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî Open approved step marks started in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**).
- **Chat-ai record action handled in Current action tracking:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** **Update in chat** **Current action tracking** when **`status === "started"`** shows **Opened for next step.** + **Record action handled for now**; **`handleMarkApprovedNextActionHandled`** persists **`completed`** + **`completed_at`** to session + signed-in **UUID** **`client_state`** ‚Äî user can mark approved step handled without leaving chat; handling request, follow-up clear, proof CRUD, Continue handoff, active-case banner, Plan, Packet, Hub, Cases, APIs, schema unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî record action handled in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**).
- **Chat-ai completed-step clarity in Current action tracking:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** when **`status === "completed"`** shows **Next action recorded as handled for now** (+ **label** when present) and **Tracking only ‚Äî not automatic filing or submission.** ‚Äî clarifies **Handled** status without leaving chat; **`handleMarkApprovedNextActionHandled`**, handling/follow-up/proof/handoff/active-case banner, Plan, Packet, Hub, Cases, APIs, schema unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Chat AI intake ‚Äî completed-step clarity in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**).
- **Packet prepared review explainer and readiness bridge:** **`/justice/packet`** **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming && !packetApproved`** emerald **Your prepared action review** card includes **`getPreparedPacketReviewExplainer`** naming **`pickPreparedNextAction`** **`stepLabel`** and **does not file or submit** copy; when signed in and **`!readyToEscalate`**, **Before you approve, finish readiness:** with **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** ‚Üí **`/justice/chat-ai`** and **Review submission draft** ‚Üí **`/justice/preview`**; **Need to fix details or add proof notes?** **Update in chat** correction line; **`handleApprovePreparedPacket`**, approval persistence, framing gates, packet body, copy/download/print, filing/tasks, APIs, schema, rules, plan, preview, chat-ai, hub, cases unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî prepared review explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/packet`)**).
- **Packet post-approval approved-step explainer:** **`/justice/packet`** when **`packetApproved && approvedNextAction?.label`**, top emerald **Your approved case packet** card uses **`getApprovedPacketNextStepExplainer`** with bold approved step / **nothing sent automatically**; **Update in chat** kept; inner approved card clarifies **Open {label}** is in-app prep/tracking not filing; **`handleApprovePreparedPacket`**, approval/**`started`**/**`completed`** persistence, framing gates, packet body, copy/download/print, filing/tasks, APIs, schema, rules, plan, preview, chat-ai, hub, cases unchanged; **no** filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action claims (¬ß2 **Packet ‚Äî post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**).
- **RLS vs Clerk:** Child-table RLS policies target Supabase Auth `uid`; app uses **Clerk id + service role** ‚Äî fine for current server-only access, confusing if client-side Supabase is introduced without redesign.
- **Analytics / profile tables** not versioned in this repo‚Äôs migrations.

---

## 7. Development workflow

1. **Branch:** Do feature work on **`cursor-dev`** (or team-agreed equivalent), not directly on `main` for risky changes.
2. **Typecheck:** Run **`npx tsc --noEmit`** before commit/PR.
3. **Test:** Exercise flows locally (intake ‚Üí preview ‚Üí plan ‚Üí cases ‚Üí evidence/tasks/filings as relevant).
4. **Commit:** Clear, scoped commits.
5. **Push** `cursor-dev` and open a **PR to `main`**.
6. **Merge** after review.
7. **Sync:** Merge or rebase **`main` back into `cursor-dev`** so the long-lived branch stays current.

Adjust branch names if the team renames them; the pattern is **integration branch ‚Üí PR ‚Üí main ‚Üí back-merge**.

---

## Document maintenance

Update this file when:

- Product north star changes.
- A new persistent subsystem is added (new tables, major routes).
- Known limitations are fixed (e.g. pagination for cases).

**Do not** duplicate every file path here forever ‚Äî link to `docs/` or code search for exhaustive inventories when needed.
